Current Affairs Commentary

Welcome Marconi to China 38

Marconi, the father of radio invention, is coming to China for a visit and will arrive in Shanghai from Nanjing today. We extend our sincere welcome to this scientist who has made great contributions to human culture. We now present.

His honorable life and his success as follows.

Marconi is Italian. He was born on April 25, 1874, in Bologna, Italy. He is sixty years old this year. He studied at Leghorn in his youth and was a prominent student of Professor Rosa. Later, he entered the University of Bologna. From that time on, he devoted himself to the study of radio.

Marconi's initial success can be considered the short-distance experiments in England in 1897. After that, some of his most honorable and memorable periods were in 1899. Wireless communication began between England and France. In 1901. The first communication across the Atlantic. In 1902. Direct communication between England and the United States and Canada. In 1904. The establishment of shipboard daily newspapers, allowing passengers at sea to receive mainland news daily. In 1910. Communication between Ireland and Argentina (5,600 miles). In 1930. Direct wireless telephone communication with Australia from the "Electra" ship in the port of Genoa, Italy, and the use of radio waves to light the electric lights in the electrical exhibition in Sydney, Australia. His most proud invention in his life was the vacuum tube. From this powerful tool, he gained infinite mysteries. He often felt that his current laboratory was not enough. He hopes to expand from this earth to the entire universe. To be used as a test to communicate with other planets.

Today, our country's scientific knowledge is truly too backward. The talent that our country needs most now is scientists. However, the future of science is limitless. The opportunities waiting for our young scientists to work hard are even greater than the opportunities for Marconi to work hard. As long as our young scientists continue to experiment diligently. Marconi has a famous saying. "I would like to tell you all that if you can do one thing wholeheartedly, you will definitely succeed." I hope that the young people of our country can keep this in mind.

A scientist's efforts in an invention must indeed rely on the great achievements left to him by his predecessors. However, modern great inventors also need a generation of young people to inherit his great success. And go a step further. To open up a new world for human culture. Today we welcome Marconi. I hope that our young scientists. Can inherit his great achievements with the spirit of Marconi's invention of radio. To benefit mankind.

Science has no nationality. The contribution of scientists. It is all over humanity. So today we welcome Marconi. It is more enthusiastic than any foreign guests. We wish Marconi's career longevity.

Henderson Visits Pang Gu to Discuss Disarmament Germany Expresses Willingness to Reach Understanding with France France Declares No Change in Disarmament Attitude 39

(Paris) This morning, Foreign Minister Pang Gu met with Henderson, Chairman of the Disarmament Conference. Mr. Henderson has recently observed the work of the Armaments Inspection and Military Quota Committees in Geneva for several days. This morning, he specially reported to Pang Gu on the results obtained by the various committees and discussed how to incorporate these results into a future general disarmament convention. In the afternoon, Pang Gu also met with Henderson, Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, and the meeting lasted from 5 pm to 6 pm, after which a communiqué was issued, stating that Pang Gu and Henderson had a long meeting, during which they discussed issues related to the Disarmament Conference and currently under discussion by all parties. Both of them believed that the work completed by the various working groups in Geneva was very beneficial. The Presidium of the Disarmament Conference believed that the issue of guaranteeing the implementation of the future disarmament convention was very important and had not been discussed by the Disarmament Conference, and specially entrusted Henderson to prepare a report on this matter. Mr. Henderson specifically sought France's opinion on this point, and Pang Gu told him everything he knew. The two then discussed the issue of continued talks between governments. (5th Havas Dispatch)

(Paris) Henderson, Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, discussed with French Foreign Minister Pang Gu today for a long time on diplomatic negotiations with Germany. It is heard that the two agreed that this secret negotiation can only be based on the declaration made by British Foreign Minister Simon in Geneva on October 14. At that time, Simon represented the major powers in declaring his firm opposition to Germany's immediate rearmament. (6th National Dispatch)

(Berlin) The British Ambassador to Germany, Sir Phipps, met with German Chancellor Hitler today to discuss disarmament issues, lasting for an hour. Hitler reiterated his eagerness to immediately reach an understanding with France. At the same time, the British Ambassador stated that the British government was very willing for France and Germany to reach a compromise on disarmament and other issues. It is heard that the German government is now waiting for the new French government to express its views on the results of the talks between the French Ambassador and Hitler. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

(Paris) Some quarters said that France's views on disarmament had changed. Since Pang Gu's meeting with Henderson today, it has proved that this news is not accurate. The French proposal has not changed the work of the Disarmament Conference at all. Pang Gu made this clear to the press tonight. Pang Gu said, "The disarmament work will continue, but it cannot go beyond the scope clearly pointed out in my recent speech in the House of Representatives." It can be seen that the saying of changing intentions is completely unfounded. (5th Havas Dispatch)

Italian Pan-System Party Congress Resolves to Fundamentally Transform the League of Nations Remaining in Geneva as a Condition Advocating Recruitment of US and Russia to Join Limiting Voting Rights of Small Countries Simplifying Meeting Procedures Not Bound by Post-War Treaties 40

Rome The Italian Pan-System Party Congress met last night, chaired by Prime Minister Mussolini. A communiqué was issued after the meeting, stating that the Pan-System Party Congress began its work in the twelfth year of the Pan-System Revolution. The Prime Minister took the opportunity to announce the Pan-System Revolutionary guidelines, which apply not only to Italy but also to the whole world. The Congress decided that Italy would remain a member of the League of Nations, but only on the condition that the League of Nations be fundamentally transformed in the shortest possible time. The so-called transformation refers to the organization, operation, and goals of the League of Nations. The Congress is scheduled to meet again tomorrow night. (6th Havas Dispatch)

Rome Today, the Fascist Congress decided that unless the League of Nations is immediately and thoroughly reorganized, Italy will follow in the footsteps of Japan and Germany and withdraw from the League of Nations. This resolution has been approved by Prime Minister Mussolini and other cabinet members. Mr. Mussolini also attended the meeting as a party member. It is heard that Italy will soon put forward specific proposals for reorganizing the League of Nations. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

Advocating Three Points of Reform 41

Rome The meeting of the Fascist Party Congress ended this morning. The Italian Prime Minister and all cabinet members attended. The meeting demanded a major revision of the League of Nations Covenant. Italy's continued membership in the League of Nations will be conditional on the purpose and status of the League of Nations being revised in the near future. Italy advocates that the League of Nations should be reformed in three ways: (1) The voting rights of small countries should be limited in matters that are only partially related to small countries; (2) The procedures of the League of Nations meetings should be simplified. Italy believes that endless discussions and the endless emergence of committees only prevent the meetings from progressing; (3) The League of Nations should not uphold the Treaty of Versailles and other similar treaties. Italy has struggled for this move, because the League of Nations has become an instrument for defending the interests of the victorious countries under British control, dividing European countries into propertied and property-less factions, so the League of Nations can only become a universal organization after a major reform. (6th National Dispatch)

Rome Last night, the Pan-System Party Congress decided that Italy would remain a member of the League of Nations, but only on the condition that the League of Nations be fundamentally transformed in the shortest possible time. This resolution was issued late at night, and political and diplomatic circles only learned of it this morning, and did not think it was very different. Regarding the substance of the reorganization of the League of Nations, Italy's claims can be briefly described as follows: Italy has always criticized the League of Nations for being too broad in scope, so it has always advocated the establishment of a system of grading countries, arguing that some major countries should occupy special positions. In addition, Italy does not want to exclude the United States and Russia and advocates seeking two ways to make it easier for the United States and Russia to accept and join the reorganized League of Nations. Italy also wants the League of Nations to have a spirit of substantial cooperation. As for the obligations of member states to the League of Nations, there should be greater freedom, so that the League of Nations does not become a judging authority, but only an advisory authority. (6th Havas Dispatch)

Strengthening Control Power 42

Rome Today, it was learned from reliable sources that Italy will invite the great powers to study the plan to reorganize the League of Nations. The main purpose of the reorganization is to strengthen the power of the League of Nations so that it becomes a truly effective institution and eliminates today's pathological state. As for the reorganization plan, it will be made into a complete plan by the General Assembly of the Fascist Party and then submitted to the League of Nations. No specific methods have been planned yet. It is heard that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini firmly believes that the soundest basis for reorganizing the League of Nations is to conclude a seven-power treaty that can control world politics. (6th National Dispatch)

Reducing the Rights of Small Countries 43

Rome Unofficial quarters predict that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini will soon make suggestions regarding the reorganization of the League of Nations. The Italian Prime Minister obviously wants to bring all the important countries that are not currently members, such as Japan, Germany, the United States, and Russia, into the League of Nations. He wants to greatly reduce the rights of small countries, because when Geneva previously discussed the Manchurian incident, small countries that had little to do with this dispute spoke a lot and occupied a very advantageous position, which Italy did not agree with. The Italian Prime Minister wants to amend Articles 10 and 19 of the League of Nations Covenant. As for expansion, the Italian Prime Minister wants to see economic expansion, including the international distribution of raw materials, because the sanction debate method contained in Article 16 can be considered immature. The above views only represent the general attitude of the Italian people. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Dissenting in Geneva 44

(Geneva) The resolution of the Fascist General Assembly was expected long ago. Some quarters believe that the General Assembly's approval of Italy's withdrawal from the League of Nations is to give Italian Prime Minister Mussolini an instrument to reorganize the League of Nations according to Italy's views. Many people sympathize with Italy's determination to revise the League of Nations Covenant, because fifteen years of experience have shown the effectiveness of the League of Nations and its weaknesses that should be improved. However, Italy's proposal to organize a supreme administrative council is not supported by people. (6th Reuters News Agency Dispatch)

Japan Severing Ties with the League of Nations Still Plans to Participate in Cultural Affairs 45

(Tokyo) After Japan officially withdrew from the League of Nations on March 27 of this year, it had originally established the general principle of completely severing relations, but later, because Dr. Tanakadate, a member of the League of Nations Cultural Committee, resigned, the League of Nations requested that a successor be sent. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs did not respond and carefully consulted with the parties concerned. Signed on the grounds that Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations was due to differing opinions on the Sino-Japanese issue, and still intends to cooperate with it in other cultural undertakings. Recently, Foreign Minister Hirota decided to find a representative figure from all parties. It has now been decided to recommend Professor Emeritus of the Imperial University, Dr. Fumizaki, as the Japanese representative to the committee, and with the approval of the person, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will notify the Secretariat of the League of Nations of the above situation within this year, and formally appoint him at the meeting of the Council next January. (6th Japanese Federation Dispatch)

British Sir Samuel Appointed Chairman of the League of Nations Aid Jewish Committee 46

Vienna The League of Nations previously sent representatives from fifteen countries to form a special committee to deal separately with the problems of Jewish refugees from Germany. The committee met today and elected British Viscount Cecil as chairman. According to High Commissioner MacDonald's estimate, there are a total of 60,000 refugees from Germany, of which 51,000 are Jews, including 25,000 who have entered France, 3,000 who have entered England, 6,500 who have entered Palestine, and 6,500 who have entered Poland. MacDonald also said that this problem can only be solved through international cooperation. (5th Reuters News Agency Dispatch)

Grand Farewell in the Italian Capital 48

Supporting the Guarantee of Peace 49

When Mr. Litvinov was about to leave, he told reporters that all elements that can guarantee peace will be approved and accepted by the Soviet Russian government, but the Russian government rejects all doubtful combinations and actions that are insufficient to promote security and peace. I have repeatedly stated in international gatherings that Soviet Russia attaches importance to "peace and security" far above any other explanation of security. All countries that hold the same purpose and maintain the same attitude can obtain the sincere cooperation of the Soviet Russian government. Mr. Litvinov also denied that the talks in Rome had other purposes besides peace, saying that the opinions he exchanged with Prime Minister Mussolini were entirely about serving the cause of peace. (5th National Dispatch)

Not a Wide Range of Topics 50

Rome Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov set off for Berlin at 8:45 tonight. The tour of Rome at the invitation of the Italian Prime Minister came to an end. After Mr. Litvinov set off, the outside world began to know that the scope of his talks with the Italian Prime Minister was not as wide as previously reported. Matters such as the Five-Power or Seven-Power Treaty were not discussed. The main achievement of this trip was the establishment of the continuation of the exchange of views between the Italian and Russian governments, rather than any practical resolution.

Italian and Russian Steps in Sync 51

The Italian Daily News, believed by many to be the mouthpiece of Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, published an article stating that Russia and Italy both want clear situations, concrete facts, and practical solutions. The two countries are willing to uphold justice in consistent and collective actions and concentrate their policies on direct relations and solutions.

Religious Compromise Still Far Away 52

The compromise between Soviet Russia and the Roman Catholic Church is still very far away. US Postmaster General Farley, who crossed the Atlantic Ocean with Litvinov, denied that he had mediated in this matter, but the Holy See did hope that Farley would explain the Soviet Russian religious concessions to the United States. Now the Holy See is quite disappointed with this explanation.

It is believed that Soviet Russia's concessions to the United States are not real. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

Italian-Russian Trade Agreement Extended 53

Rome Representatives of Italy and Russia signed a document today in the Corporation Ministry, extending the commercial agreement between Italy and Russia and stipulating that it will remain in effect until 1934. According to this agreement, which was signed on May 6 of this year, it contains two treaties. The first treaty stipulates that all goods from both countries shall enjoy most-favored-nation treatment in accordance with the principle of reciprocity. The first treaty stipulates that the Italian government shall lend Soviet Russia up to 200,000,000 lire, so that it can buy goods in Italy. With the consent of both parties in the future, this number can still be increased. (5th Havas Dispatch)

Rome Regarding the Italian-Russian tariff treaty, the Standing Committee of the House of Representatives for the Study of Commercial Treaty Issues has prepared a report and distributed it to the members for their reading. Its content explains that the summary of trade between Italy and Russia is beneficial to the Soviet Union. The conclusion is that although the amount of trade between the two countries cannot be required to be completely equal, the difference between them should eventually be made as small as possible. (5th Havas Dispatch)

Purpose of the Trip to Italy 54

Rome Soviet Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov explained to the foreign press the purpose of his visit to Rome. Mr. Litvinov first stated that the purpose of this official visit was neither to change the existing diplomatic relations between Italy and Russia nor to seek new cooperation methods or compromises that are harmful to other countries. Mr. Litvinov said that fortunately, Italy and Russia have not only had no conflicts in the past ten years, but have never even had disagreements. Mr. Litvinov continued, "However, in addition to the interests directly related to Italy and Russia, there are still many international issues that we cannot ignore. These issues are increasing day by day and disputes are becoming more and more serious." The purpose of Mr. Litvinov's visit was to personally contact Italian Prime Minister Mussolini on these issues so as to study the attitudes that the two governments should take towards these issues. After exchanging views, it was proved that the policies of the two countries have many similarities. Mr. Litvinov also said that the Soviet Russian government always seeks ways to maintain peace when observing international issues. All plans that can guarantee peace can be approved or participated in by the Soviet Russian government. "Therefore, all those who love peace should not have doubts about the Soviet Russian diplomatic actions and the exchanges of its diplomatic representatives." Soviet Russia has recently conducted various diplomatic talks, on the one hand seeking to consolidate the relations between Soviet Russia, France, the United States, and Italy, and on the other hand maintaining general peace. Mr. Litvinov's visit to Rome this time is a scene of this kind of talk.

Russian-German Relations 55

Then a reporter asked him about the German incident. Mr. Litvinov replied that he had met with German Foreign Minister Neurath in Berlin before going to the United States. When he returns to Moscow, he plans to pass through Vienna, but it is not yet known whether he will stay there. Someone asked him if he had considered the issue of Italian mediation in German-Russian relations when he met with Mussolini. Mr. Litvinov replied, "Since there is a direct relationship between Soviet Russia and Germany, why use Italy as an intermediary?"

Good Neighborliness Policy 56

Another reporter asked for his opinion on the relations between the Soviet Russian and Little Entente countries. Mr. Litvinov said that Soviet Russia is prepared to restore diplomatic relations with all countries. In addition, Mr. Litvinov also said that during his stay in Rome, he had no contact with the Vatican because Soviet Russia's domestic affairs are separate from church and state. A reporter asked him if he had mentioned the Vatican when talking with Mussolini. Mr. Litvinov replied, "We talked about everything."

The Question of Japan 57

When reporters asked about the Japanese issue, the answer was the same. Regarding the League of Nations, Mr. Litvinov declared that Soviet Russia did not intend to participate in this meeting. When talking about the Disarmament Conference, Mr. Litvinov said that this meeting had become a corpse, and said that whether disarmament can be realized depends not on the method used but on whether all parties have the will to disarm.

No Hope for Disarmament 58

He said, "Only when all countries are willing to implement the Kellogg-Briand Pact in good faith can there be hope for disarmament, but today, when some countries are still talking about war and still preparing for war, how can the disarmament issue be successful?"

Brewing War 59

Someone asked if, in his opinion, there was a possibility of war breaking out soon. Mr. Litvinov replied, "Since war machines already exist, how can war not be possible?" (5th Havas Dispatch)

British-Made Textile Machinery Imported to Japan: A Total Value of Ten Million Pounds in Twelve Years 60

(London) Commerce Secretary Runciman stated in the House of Commons today, in response to a question from a Member of Parliament, that in the twelve years from 1921 to 1932, British textile machinery imported to Japan, Taiwan, and Kwantung was worth a total of 14,333,200 pounds. At the same time, exports of other types of machinery were worth 14,859,900 pounds. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

Page 7

A Reuters correspondent learned in the House of Commons smoking room that if de Valera makes further requests to the British government, it will inform him that the door to a final solution remains open. However, he must genuinely aim for a final solution and be in accordance with the British response. As for the British government's attitude towards the financial situation, it will depend on the nature and scope of the negotiations. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

(London) According to the remarks made by Dominion Secretary Thomas in the House of Commons this afternoon, the British government does not wish to send an ultimatum to the Irish Free State, so the door to a satisfactory resolution remains open. Today, the Members' seats and the public gallery were both packed. Free State High Commissioner Dulanty and South African High Commissioner Walter were also present. Thomas today explained the British government's reasons for not responding to the Irish Free State's request for its attitude should South Africa declare a republic. He first read a letter from Irish Executive Council President de Valera, stating that Thomas's remarks in the House of Commons on November 14, asking the House to pay attention to the three bills proposed by the Free State Parliament, were in conflict with the Anglo-Irish Treaty. He also expressed the British government's hope that the Free State would remain a part of the British Empire and willingly accept its responsibilities and enjoy its privileges. De Valera then refuted this, stating that the Irish people had never wished to be a part of the British Empire and that their union with Britain and the British Empire had never been voluntary. They had always wished to maintain their right to be an independent nation. Their submission to British rule in any form was due to oppression by superior power and was not their wish. The Anglo-Irish Treaty of 1921 did not fundamentally change Ireland's attitude, and the Irish people did not regard it as a final solution to Anglo-Irish relations or recognize that it gave Britain the right to interfere in the constitutional development of Ireland. The Free State government inferred from Thomas's remarks on November 14 that the British government now also knew the harm of forced union and would not regard Ireland's decision to secede from the British Empire as a reason for war or other acts of aggression. This attitude of the British government should be formed in a direct communication.

Thomas's reply stated that the British government could not accept the description of the relationship between the two countries in the letter. He then stated his views on the 1921 Treaty as stated in his public letter of April 1932, as follows:

"The British government's establishment of the 1921 Treaty was with a simple desire, which was to end the long-standing animosity between the two countries from then on. The British government is confident that this resolution has created a peace and satisfaction that no other method could achieve. Furthermore, the Free State has thus been able to participate in the significant constitutional developments of the past few years, especially the status of the Dominions and Britain as members of the British Empire under the Crown, which is a practical provision and is recognized by the world. This is also a direct result of the 1921 settlement."

Thomas's reply also pointed out that the 1921 Treaty was formally recognized by the elected representatives of the Irish people, and subsequent Free State general elections added to this recognition. During the period from 1921 to 1932, there was much development in friendship and cooperation between the two countries. He continued that the British government could not accept the assumption that permanent friendship could not be established based on the current relationship, so it did not see any reason to answer questions based on this assumption. The British government did not believe that the Free State government was trying to renounce its treaty obligations in the manner indicated in the letter. Therefore, the British government did not wish to explain its intended attitude in what it considered to be purely hypothetical circumstances. Under this treaty, the Free State already enjoyed the freedom to interact on an equal footing with other members of the British Empire. The British government felt that this interaction was ironclad proof of Ireland's free development of its own future within the British Empire. The natural union between Britain and Ireland was necessary for their complete prosperity. The British government had always sincerely wished to manage affairs with the Free State in a friendly and cooperative manner as a member of the British Empire. Opposition leader Lansbury asked whether other members of the British Empire could be consulted. Thomas replied that the dispute arose because the Free State denied its Anglo-Irish treaty obligations, so this was a matter between Britain and Ireland. He did not wish to involve other Dominions. The British government's intention was not to close the door to an honorable resolution. If other Dominions were consulted, then other Dominions would be affected. He hoped that this situation would not occur. If it did, he would inform the House in detail. However, he wished speakers not to make remarks that would only make the situation more serious. Before Thomas read the letters, a Member of Parliament asked whether it would be possible to make the people of the Free State living in Britain and the Free State aware of the disadvantages in their status and entry into Britain after the Free State declared a republic. Thomas replied that he did not feel that it was necessary to take this step yet. He hoped that this situation would never materialize. The privileges enjoyed by the people of the British Empire in Britain were different from those of foreigners. This was well known. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

German Government Issues Declaration on the Jewish Question: Jewish Influence in Germany Is Enormous; Dealing With It Is Related to Survival 61

(Berlin) German Interior Minister Frick today issued an important declaration on the question of dealing with Jews, stating that the National Socialist Party's laws on racial issues are based on the principle of preserving racial purity. This is of the utmost importance to the future survival of the German nation. The same principle has also been put into practice in other countries, especially in Asian countries. However, in Germany, the foreign people who occupy the greatest power are the Jews. Although the number of Jews in Germany is only 1.5% of the total population, since the last ten years or so, especially since 1918, they have been successively moving into Germany from Eastern Europe. They have come to wield enormous power in the German economic, financial, cultural, and political spheres, far exceeding their numbers. For example, in Prussia alone, of the total of 11,814 lawyers, Jews account for 3,515, which is 29.8% of the total. Furthermore, as for public registrars, Jewish people account for 1,945 of the 6,226, which is 31.2%. If we consider the position of Jewish people in German universities, the composition is even more astonishing. Approximately 30% of ordinary professors are Jewish. In the medical departments of the Universities of Breslau and Berlin, Jewish professors occupy 45% of the total. This excessive expansion of foreign people has become an urgent issue for the survival of the German nation. Therefore, Germany's racial laws are based only on the principle of self-preservation and do not involve racial hatred. Today, the German government's goal is to preserve the traditional German concepts of the German state, and can thus protect racial purity. But this does not mean that the German government has the right to judge foreign nationalities. The German government is well aware that many of the foreign people in Germany represent ancient and highly civilized peoples. Therefore, the German government and people do not dare to despise the inherent value and contributions of other nationalities. At present, foreign people residing in Germany can still live and work in peace, and German schools continue to accept the children of foreign people. Given the importance of the German nation's self-preservation, other countries also have this kind of assertion. Therefore, when Germany receives requests from various countries and regions to deal with racial issues, marriage issues, etc. as soon as possible, the German government is greatly surprised. If other countries arbitrarily spread rumors about Germany's national legal system, then apart from being based on false and incomplete hearsay, it is a malicious slander against Germany. (5th National Telegraph)

Indian-Japanese Conference: Indian Side's Attitude Is Firm; Japanese Private Representatives Prepare to Return Home 62

New Delhi Japanese private representatives, including Bing Shang and Ono, believing that the Indian-Japanese trade conference has no hope of success, withdrew from the meeting today and will return home within the week. According to sources close to the Indian representatives, the Indian side's firm attitude is due to: (1) India wants to revise existing trade treaties with other countries, so it wants to obtain the most favorable terms possible in the Indian-Japanese conference so that it can serve as a basis for future conferences with other countries. (2) Japanese textile manufacturers and cotton merchants are unwilling to make any concessions, which has created a bad impression on the Indian people, so they are also unwilling to compromise. (3) The British House of Commons is taking a hostile attitude towards Japan in industry and commerce. (6th National Telegraph)

Soviet Russian Plan to Develop Siberia: Seventeen Hydroelectric Power Stations to Be Built Within Ten Years; Widespread Construction of Factories and Railways to Become Electrified 65

(Moscow) Eastern Siberia is rich in resources. The Angara and Yenisei Rivers have a power generation potential of 185 million kilowatts, and there are large deposits of minerals such as tungsten, gold, other precious metals, tin, lead, copper, iron, and coal reserves of approximately 28.5 billion tons. The huge plan to develop this region (the so-called Angara-Yenisei Great Plan) was drawn up by some of the Soviet Union's most famous scientists. Its implementation period will be from ten to fifteen years. According to this plan, seventeen hydroelectric power stations will be built on the Yenisei and Angara Rivers, with a total power generation capacity of 73 million kilowatts. Various factories will be built around these power stations, such as factories for manufacturing artificial rubber, artificial dyes, and various mining factories. The area is also rich in wood, so paper and pulp mills and other textile industrial enterprises will be set up. In 1934, woodworking factories, paper mills, and wood manufacturing plants will be built first. If eastern Siberia is fully developed, it will be able to supply 50% to 55% of the Soviet Union's national demand for ferrous alloys and electric steel, as well as 50% of lead. At the same time, the plan also stipulates that at the beginning of the third five-year plan, the electrification of the Great Siberian Railway from Moscow to the Pacific will be completed using the electricity from the region. (TASS Dispatch, 4th)

Roosevelt Announces End of Prohibition; Also Asks People to Drink Moderately; Dry Faction Makes Last-Ditch Effort; Foreign Wine Imports and Taverns Reopen; Drinkers Celebrate Frantically 66

(Washington) The American experiment with Prohibition officially ended at 6:55 p.m. today, with the U.S. President issuing a proclamation repealing the Eighteenth Amendment to the Constitution, which stipulated Prohibition. At the same time, he also announced the immediate abolition of several additional special taxes levied in the recovery plan for gasoline, capital, and bonuses. This special tax can generate 225,000,000 yuan annually. Now that it has been compensated by the liquor tax, it is abolished immediately to relieve the people's hardships. When announcing the end of Prohibition, the U.S. President also asked the people of the country to exercise self-restraint and not to indulge in drinking, to purchase alcohol from licensed taverns, to help the government eliminate smugglers, and to increase tax revenue. He also asked the states not to restore the old taverns. As Prohibition was lifted, the Alcohol Import Commission immediately announced that the first allocation of import quotas for liquor from various countries had been drafted and licenses could be obtained and imports transported immediately. The quotas set were not announced. The International Reform Alliance, which has always been the strongest advocate of Prohibition, is still making a last-ditch effort to recognize that the ratification of the Twenty-First Amendment to the Constitution by the National Conventions of States did not comply with constitutional procedures. It appealed to the Supreme Court of the District of Columbia to prevent the Undersecretary of State from formally announcing the end of Prohibition, but it was rejected today by Judge Ray. Officials estimate that the American brewing industry is now selling 60 million yuan in stocks to expand its business. (5th National Telegraph)

"Re-Entry into Paradise" New Drink; Tavern Owner's Commemorative Idea 67

(New York) Last night, countless people celebrated the repeal of Prohibition in major hotels. In one large hotel, a tavern owner, 82 years old, happily returned to his old business and combined French-produced wines with a drink called "Re-Entry into Paradise" to commemorate the occasion. Commemorative texts in newspapers on the opening of Prohibition occupied important space. For example, the front eleven pages of the "New York Evening Post" and the front six pages of the "New York Times" were filled with alcohol advertisements. The situation was similar in other newspapers. (5th Havas Dispatch)

Making Wooden Idols and Burning Them; Actions of American Residents in Paris Are Particularly Interesting 68

(Paris) The newspaper Le Journal reported that American expatriates enthusiastically celebrated the end of Prohibition. Many wine shops held "wet festivals." For example, in a wine shop on the Champs-Élysées, a wooden puppet representing "Prohibition," resembling an evil woman, as tall as a person, was displayed and then burned. Such particularly interesting actions occurred everywhere. (6th Havas Dispatch)

(3) To ask the provincial government to designate the provincial bank to issue circulating notes, etc., to collect back the paper money, with the assets of the money shops and local arrears of additional taxes as collateral. (4) To order the shareholders of the Gongyu Company to be fully responsible for redemption, and to recommend representatives from the county party headquarters, farmers' associations, and chambers of commerce to go to the province with Wu Gengyu of the provincial committee and County Magistrate She Nianci to appeal, requesting permission to implement the third method. Negotiations Still Pending for the Takeover of Yuguan: Japanese Still Occupying Dongluocheng Inside the Pass; Iwai Arrives in Beiping to Negotiate with Huang and He; No Intention of Withdrawal from Pseudo-Army in Malanyu 119

Beiping Correspondence: Regarding the issue of taking over the passes along the Great Wall, although the Japanese have declared they will return them, they are still creating many obstacles. For example, regarding the takeover of Shanhaiguan, the Japanese had previously agreed that the North China military and political authorities would send Tao Shangming and Zhu Shiqin, accompanied by a military attaché from the Japanese embassy, to Yuguan to negotiate the takeover procedures. After Tao and others arrived in Yuguan, they consulted with Endo, the staff officer of the 14th Mixed Brigade of the Japanese Army, and Iwai, the newly appointed head of the Yuguan Special Affairs Agency, on all matters. Unexpectedly, the Japanese then proposed to build barracks and open markets in Dongluocheng (inside the Great Wall), a place four or five li outside the east gate of Yuguan County, moving all the pseudo-organizations and pseudo-police inside Yuguan City to that location. At the time, Tao and others believed that Dongluocheng was inside the Great Wall and close to Yuguan City, which was not in line with the principle of taking over the passes, and feared that the close proximity would easily lead to disputes. This was outside the scope of their mission and authority, and they could not make a decision. Subsequently, they telegraphed the authorities for instructions, and it was also deemed a major issue, and it was advocated that it be discussed at length and temporarily shelved, resulting in the Yuguan meeting ending without result.

After the Yuguan meeting, Tao and others went to various counties in eastern Luan to inspect, while the Japanese, without waiting for our consent, immediately started construction in Dongluocheng. In recent days, a portion of the project has been completed. The Japanese also sent Iwai, the head of their Yuguan Special Affairs Agency, to Beiping for negotiations. Yesterday, Iwai arrived in Beiping with Tao Shangming, and in the afternoon, guided by Tao, paid respects to Huang Fu and He Yingqin to make diplomatic greetings. Then, they had a lengthy discussion on the issue of taking over Yuguan. According to Iwai's statement to our side, the Japanese use of Dongluocheng is temporary, for the convenience of relocating the garrison and various agencies of the puppet state. Currently, the barracks and agency buildings are under construction, and will be completed in two weeks, at which time the Japanese army will relocate and the various agencies of the puppet state will also move, and the takeover of Yuguan can be realized simultaneously. However, it is heard that the Japanese army's construction there is intended for long-term occupation, which our side will find difficult to recognize. Therefore, the negotiations in Beiping have not yet yielded satisfactory results. It has been decided that Iwai will return to Yuguan tonight (the 3rd) at 8:00 PM. The counties in eastern Luan, Yuguan, and various passes have not been taken over and are also being ravaged by bandits. For example, the area around Funing is scarred. The order has gradually been restored in Qian'an, Lulong, and Changli counties. The area east of the Shi River is still within the sphere of influence of Japanese and Korean ronin and cannot be rectified. Yin Shousong, the magistrate of Linyu County, has been dismissed by the provincial government for ineffective handling of affairs, and Yuan Tai has been appointed to take over. The discipline of the Liu Zuozhou unit of the security team reorganized from Li Jichun's troops is poor, and the provincial government has also issued strict orders for rectification. Since Malanyu was occupied by Japanese and puppet troops on October 22, although our side has negotiated with the Japanese side, and the Japanese side has stated that they will withdraw immediately, there is still no sign of withdrawal. A Japanese regiment is stationed there, led by Captain Hirasawa Kiichi. Three companies of puppet troops are stationed, one in Tashan, one in Dongling, and one in Tashan School. The Japanese and puppet troops stationed there claim to be protecting the imperial tombs, but in reality, they are actively building barracks and purchasing more than ten mu of civilian land to build a large-scale airfield, with the intention of making the area an air force base to control North China. (December 3rd) Da

Feng Yuxiang's Guards Returned to Chahar Province; Financial Difficulties Lead to Austerity; Only a Small Number Remain in the Mountains as Guards; Liu and Zhang Arrive in Shandong to Negotiate Northern Transportation 120

Jinan Correspondence: Feng Yuxiang fought against the Japanese in Chahar, but did not achieve his ambition. Due to circumstances, he left Chahar and came south again, settling in Mount Tai. Song Zheyuan had dispatched a portion of his 29th Army, about 3,000 men, to escort Feng to Mount Tai, stationed on the mountain and in Taian County. The cavalry battalion of Sun Tongxuan's 20th Division of Han Fuju's 3rd Route Army, which was originally stationed in the area, was relocated to Dawenkou due to the arrival of Feng's guards in Mount Tai. At the beginning of Feng's arrival in Mount Tai, the finances were very difficult. Although Song Zheyuan and Han Fuju occasionally provided assistance, it was not enough in reality. Therefore, the troops in Mount Tai had no salary other than daily meals. Even Feng's key personnel received only twenty yuan a month for living expenses. Feng's financial straits being as such, he had no choice but to cut expenses to maintain the status quo. Last month, Feng had dismissed more than 400 soldiers stationed in Mount Tai, transported them to Jinan, and given each person two yuan to return to their hometown. Recently, Feng decided that since there were still about 2,000 soldiers stationed in Mount Tai, and it was difficult to pay them, and he himself was reading books in the mountains and did not ask about politics, there was no need for so many troops. Therefore, he decided to leave only a very small number in Mount Tai to serve as guards, and return the rest to Chahar Province. Therefore, he telegraphed Song Zheyuan a few days ago, urging him to send someone to Mount Tai to take command of the troops stationed in Mount Tai and return them to Chahar.

After receiving the telegram, Song Zheyuan sent Liu Ruming and Zhang Zhizhong to Shandong to handle the matter, and telegraphed Feng in Taian and Han Fuju in Jinan. Liu and Zhang arrived in Jinan this morning (4th) by train from Beiping at 8:15 PM. After getting off the train, Liu and Zhang first went to the municipal government to rest and met with Feng's secretary, Li Xin. Then, they went to the provincial government to meet with Han Fuju to convey Song Zheyuan's intentions and discuss the transportation of the troops stationed in Mount Tai. Tomorrow morning (5th), they will take a train to Mount Tai to meet Feng. It is estimated that the troops stationed in Mount Tai will be transported to Chahar soon. (4th)

Communist Party Deceives a Group of People - Zou Chunsheng's Confession 123

Since Chairman Chiang Kai-shek personally led the national army to supervise the suppression of communist bandits, in view of the fact that not all members of the Communist Party are stubborn and incorrigible, and that many are forced to join, he decided to use seven parts political force and only three parts military force as the decisive strategy for eliminating communist bandits. Since its implementation, not only has military progress been made step by step, but the use of political force has also been very effective. Therefore, many young people in the Communist Party have become self-aware and surrendered, as has been repeatedly reported in newspapers. Now, the Communist Zou Chunsheng has also surrendered and published an account of his joining the Communist Party and a declaration of leaving the Communist Party, which shows a glimpse of the Communist Party's deception of the people under false pretenses. The following is a transcript:

Joining Process 124

"In 1926, the Revolutionary Army arrived in Jiangxi, and I joined the Communist Party. In 1927, I was transferred back to Gaoan (my county) to serve as the county party secretary. After the failure of the Nanchang Uprising, I fled to the countryside. (My family) hid me in the countryside for two years. During these two years, I suffered the misfortune of family ruin and death (my mother died for me). At that time, I was young and impulsive, which led to a manic illness. After half a year of recovery, I came to Beiping in 1927 to take the entrance exam for the Chinese University. I looked everywhere for the Communist Party organization, but after several months, there was still no organizational relationship. I gave up my studies and secretly worked as a rickshaw puller for several months. In 1930, when the Jiang-Yan War broke out, Yang (?) introduced me to the Committee Against Warlord Infighting. Later, I was discovered by the authorities when I presided over a mass rally against warlord infighting. That night, I was arrested in my apartment and taken to the Public Security Bureau. After two months, I was transferred to the Guard Command. After three months, I was interrogated several times in the Guard Department. Later, because Yan Xishan escaped, I was released from prison. After being released from prison, my emotions became more agitated and my actions became more active. Yang introduced me to the Communist Party again. Not long after joining the party, I served as the secretary of the Chinese University branch, and then as the secretary of the Anti-Imperialist Party Group in Beiping. In March 1931, (?) I served as the secretary of the Eastern District Committee of the Communist Party. In July, I fled to Shanghai after the authorities discovered me (introduced by the Communist Party). After arriving in Shanghai, I could not find an organization because the Communist Party contact was not working well. In October, I risked returning to Beiping. After returning to Beiping, I became a worker again. Soon after, I served as the Minister of Workers of the Beiping Municipal Committee of the Communist Party, and later as the Secretary of the Beiping Municipal Committee of the Communist Party, concurrently serving as the Provincial Workers' Committee of the Communist Party in Hebei. In July 1932, I was transferred to serve as the Secretary of the Tianjin Municipal Committee of the Communist Party (at this time, I became a key central cadre of the Communist Party in Hebei). In November 1932, after Huang Ping, a communist, came to Tianjin to inspect the labor movement and was arrested, I was sent back to Beiping. At first, I served as a staff member of the Organization Department of the Hebei Provincial Committee of the Communist Party (I actually took on the task of the minister due to the illness of the organization minister). Later, I served as the chairman of the Training Committee of the Hebei Provincial Committee (this work is extremely important in the Communist Party). Later, I served as a roving commissioner of the Hebei Provincial Committee. After the Zhangjiakou Incident, the central representative of the Communist Party felt that the Zhangjiakou Communist Party Forward Committee was politically weak, so I was immediately transferred to Zhangjiakou to serve as the Provincial Committee (serving as the secretary and organization minister in the Forward Committee). After the failure of Zhangjiakou, I left with the team. During this encirclement of the team, I left the team with difficulty due to my responsibility. I arrived in Beiping on October 18th. I was arrested that day. After being arrested, I deeply felt the fundamental error of the Communist Party's understanding of the Chinese revolution. I asked the authorities to give me a new life. Later, I was given a new life by the authorities who did not pursue the past. Today, I have obtained the path of self-renewal and vow to stand under the leadership of the Three Principles of the People and work to complete the national revolution. Zou Chunsheng

Declaration of Leaving the Party 125

"Comrades of the Chinese Communist Party, fellow compatriots, I, who have been deceived by the Communist Party for many years, now declare that I am breaking away from all relations with the Communist Party and faithfully standing under the leadership of the Three Principles of the People, resolutely doing anti-communist work and fighting to complete the revolution. My resolute departure from the Communist Party this time is definitely not out of fear of death and seeking life, selling the party and seeking glory, nor is it like the comrades of the Communist Party who are now coldly laughing and scolding that 'Old Zou is a traitor to the proletariat.' 'Old Zou will always be an enemy of the revolution,' nor is it like what friends are laughing at, 'How can weak-willed Old Zou do the work of the Communist Party?' Comrades of the Communist Party, dear friends, my departure this time is because I am faithful to the revolution and carry out my oath to stand on the side of the people to seek the liberation of the people. My transformation this time is the result of my long-term pain and practical life in pursuing the fundamental problem of the Chinese revolution, and it is from the political perspective that a new awareness has emerged. That is, my deep exploration of the policies and actions implemented by the Communist Party for the Chinese revolution makes it impossible for me to follow the Communist Party blindly. The Chinese Communist Party's fundamental misunderstanding of the Chinese revolution and the unsuitability of communism for China, these basic issues, can be seen at a glance by anyone who understands Chinese history, politics, and social conditions. China is a fragmented country, and all phenomena from primitive to modern exist in a complex society. The entire nation is in a state of poverty, externally suffering from imperialist aggression and internally suffering from the disasters of feudal forces. The power of China's new industry is like finding a needle in a haystack, and the future development of national capital is constantly being hit by the above two reactionary forces, making Chinese society still in a semi-colonial and feudal hell. At present, the requirements of the Chinese state and society are to strive for equal international status, realize democratic politics, and eliminate the overall poverty of the Chinese people. Then, the basic task of the Chinese revolution at present is to overthrow imperialism, overthrow feudal forces, and strive for production and construction. This is the basic understanding of the Chinese revolution. However, the Chinese Communist Party, in order to be loyal to Red Imperialism and seek help from the Third International, has brought unworkable communism to China to practice, and inhuman policies to China to act. What class struggle and Soviet revolution are nothing but a thorough destruction of society, making the Chinese people forever trapped in poverty and exile beyond remedy, and making China move from a semi-colonial state to destruction. If we talk about the political line of the Chinese Communist Party being correct, then why did Chen Duxiu's opportunism, Li Lisan's adventurism, and Qu Qiubai's reconciliationism emerge? These phenomena are all the sins of Chen, Li, and Qu, but they prove that everything that the Chinese Communist Party has implemented in China is unworkable. Saying that the Chinese Communist Party is leading the people to overthrow imperialism is even more of a laughing matter. Since the September 18th Incident, the crisis of the Chinese nation has become more urgent day by day. At this critical juncture of national survival, the Chinese Communist Party is implementing a conspiracy to destroy the national united front and sacrifice national interests. Every time Japanese imperialist aircraft and cannons launch a fierce offensive, the Communist Party carries out destructive work on the front and rear lines of the anti-Japanese war. In the rear, they direct the Red Army to 'attack the route' and under the slogan of 'expanding the Soviet area,' they fiercely attack the national army, preventing the national army from being transferred north to resist Japan. On the front line, they organize mutinies in the national army, and in Beiping, Tianjin, and Tangshan, they incite general strikes by workers, and in eastern Hebei, they arrange peasant uprisings, attempting to disrupt the anti-Japanese battlefield and disperse the anti-Japanese forces of the national army and the people. The Zhangjiakou Incident was caused by the Hebei Communist Party using Feng Yuxiang to split the anti-Japanese forces, so that the Kuomintang Central Government could not go all out to resist Japan. Even more shamefully, they use the name of fake anti-Japanese war, on the one hand, to incite the people and soldiers to oppose the Kuomintang and the Nanjing government, and on the other hand, to collude with Japan to seize Beiping, Tianjin, and North China. Compatriots from all walks of life, how can we talk about going all out to resist Japan as long as the Communist Party exists? Some people say that the Communist Party is seeking the interests of the working people. This is another shameless propaganda of the Communist Party to the people. The Communist Party's labor movement, peasant movement, soldier movement, and student movement are nothing but bloodless means of killing people by the Communist Party. It incites workers to conduct unconscious strikes, resulting only in workers losing their jobs and being arrested. It incites peasants to resist rent and taxes for no reason, and even incites peasants to arm themselves and carry out riots, destroying the countryside, resulting in families being broken up, fleeing, and losing their lives. It incites anti-Japanese soldiers to go on strike and carry out mutinies in order to fulfill its conspiracy to destroy the anti-Japanese war and save the country. But the result is that the soldiers are either shot or have no way to survive. General young students are deceived by the Communist Party due to their patriotic enthusiasm, and as a result, they have not achieved patriotism but have become a sacrifice of the Communist Party. What kind of thing is the sacred and inviolable Soviet revolution? Let's take a look at the so-called Soviet area. The Soviet area is truly a hell on earth, an irredeemable mundane world. The scene in the Soviet area is only to see fields abandoned, young and old are separated, and young men are forced to become soldiers under the Communist Party's slogan of 'expanding' 'expanding a million iron Red Army' and become cannon fodder for the Communist Party. Beautiful girls are helplessly living the life of one woman and ten thousand men under the coercion of the Communist Party. The shameless Communist Party also says that it organizes women's nursing comfort teams for the revolution. Comrades of the Chinese Communist Party, you must resolutely liberate yourselves from the myth of the Soviet Union! Regarding the darkness in the Communist Party, that is a thousand layers upon layers. I hope that the comrades of the Communist Party will examine themselves. As a result of the examination, you will know what kind of life you are living in the Communist Party now. Comrades of the Chinese Communist Party, fellow compatriots, the national crisis is now imminent. The land of China is about to be cut up by imperialist robbers. It is a time of deep water and hot fire, which cannot be remedied. Let us unite, unite under the leadership of the Three Principles of the People, and fight to complete the national revolution. Zou Chunsheng (Central News Agency)

Xuzhou Citizens' Congress Holds Publicity for Punishing Traitors and Incinerates Private Paper Currency 126

The situation is recorded as follows:

Citizens' Congress 127

For publicity on punishing traitors, the county party department first stipulated that the 5th to the 11th be publicity week. The citizens' congress was held on the morning of the 5th, and slogans were posted throughout the city. The party committee chairman, Tan Minghua, reported on the course of the Fujian Incident and the significance of punishing traitors. Subsequently, Rui Zhenxiang of the party committee proposed three motions: (1) To telegraph the Central Party Headquarters and the National Government to send troops to punish the traitors; (2) To telegraph condolences to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and all the officers and soldiers suppressing the bandits; (3) To telegraph the Executive Yuan to clean up the paper currency. The draft telegram was read out and unanimously passed. Publicity work will be carried out separately after the meeting. It is planned that the provincial civil education hall will hold a speech on suppressing bandits and punishing traitors on the 6th, and the provincial civil education hall will conduct publicity on suppressing bandits and punishing traitors in the implementation area on the 7th. On the 8th, items to comfort the officers and soldiers will be collected. On the 9th, the schools will guide the student associations to conduct speeches and competitions on punishing traitors and suppressing bandits. On the 10th, the comforting items will be announced.

Boy Scout Inspection 128

The local county's Boy Scout troop, with a history of fifteen years, was registered as Party Boy Scouts after the Northern Expedition of the Kuomintang to implement party indoctrination. Now, the third inspection is being held. The Provincial Boy Scout Council has sent Executive Director Chen Bangcai to Xuzhou for inspection and training. The participating Boy Scout troops include: Troop 669 of Xuzhou Women's Normal School, Troop 45 of Xuzhou Middle School, Troop 518 of Tongshan Normal School, Troop 631 of Private Xuzhou School, Troop 665 of Xuzhou Middle School Experimental Elementary School, Troop 666 of Women's Normal School Experimental Elementary School, Troop 886 of Private Zhongzheng School, Troop 692 of Zhongshan Street, Troop 691 of Wenchang Street, Troop 348 of Daxiangkou, and the two troops of Tongshan Experimental Elementary School and Zhengxin Elementary School, totaling twelve troops with 546 people. The troops were arranged in formation. Chen, along with Jin Shuzhi and Wang Xinmin, representatives of the 7th Division, Tan Minghua and Rui Zhengxiang, representatives of the Party Headquarters, She Nianzi, the county magistrate, and Liu Tianzhan, the director of the Education Bureau, etc., conducted an inspection. Zhang Tao, the coach of Xuzhou Middle School, was the general commander and performed basic movements and marching formations. Then Chen gave a speech, urging them to be pure Boy Scouts, to become good students in school, good children in their families, and good citizens of the country. Finally, souvenirs were distributed.

Burning of Paper Money 129

The private banknotes that had been withdrawn due to the bank run in Xuzhou Port were burned in the county government a few days ago in the first batch. Today, the second batch is being burned. County Magistrate She Nianci reported on the process of handling the currency run. Since the bank run, a three-week restriction on cash withdrawals was implemented to benefit the poor. Now, the withdrawals have been stopped for settlement. It was decided to strictly pursue and investigate the assets of the paper money merchants to prevent the common people from suffering losses. Subsequently, representatives from all walks of life checked the number of banknotes to ensure they matched, then they were poured with kerosene and set ablaze. The amount included 130,000 strings from Gongyu, 11,150 strings from Buxinji, 12,775 strings from Shixingchang, 13,450 strings from Juhechang, 9,850 strings from Chunquan, 2,000 strings from Yizhenxiang, and 5,500 strings from Tianbaoyu, totaling 184,725 strings. After the fire was reported, thick smoke billowed, and the onlookers cheered. (5th day)

Ruffians in Nanhui Chop Three People to Death with Axes 130

Zhao Shunsheng, a farmer from Jiangjialu Town, Nanhui County, had a grudge against the ruffian Zhou Huojin and others due to monetary disputes. At 2:00 AM the day before yesterday, Zhou Huojin suddenly led Xiaobeijing and Titousiwu, among four or five others, rushed to his house, each wielding sharp axes, and started chopping randomly at anyone they saw. Zhao Shunsheng was chopped to death in the kitchen. Zhao's eldest son, Longxiang, managed to escape, but was chased and chopped to death by Xiaobeijing by the river. Zhao's wife, Huang, and second son, Linxiang, and daughter, Guizhen, were also seriously injured. Huang died soon after. After committing the crime, the murderers fled one after another. Later, Zhu Genshan, an investigation police officer from the Public Security Bureau, in coordination with the 2nd District Security Corps, searched in all directions. Zhou Huojin was captured yesterday morning in a graveyard west of the town. Xiaobeijing fled to Chuansha in the afternoon and was detained by the 5th District Security Corps of that county. The 2nd District Security Corps of this county was notified to send personnel to escort him back to the corps. The 2nd District Office reported the criminals to the county for interrogation, and the county committee sent an adjudicator to conduct an inquest on the victims' bodies today (5th day).

Finance Department Approves Reduction of Tax Rates 131

This county has suffered unusually severe disasters this year, and the autumn harvest is poor. The county government has already drafted a proposal to reduce tax rates and submitted it to the Finance Department for approval. The department sent a committee member to Nanhui to conduct an on-site inspection. It is now known that the county government has been ordered to approve an 80% reduction in taxes on paddy fields, a 58% reduction in taxes on old reeds, and a complete exemption from taxation for newly enclosed and unenclosed areas, as well as new reeds in the first district.

Bullets Found in Mailbox in Songjiang 132

During the current winter defense period, the military and police agencies have been conducting strict patrols of the city and countryside, and the local area is considered peaceful. However, at 7:00 AM on the 6th, when the Liguan Post Office in this city opened for business, two rifle bullets were found in the post office mailbox. Where they came from and what the intention was is a matter of great concern. The bureau had previously been robbed of a large sum of money, and there is concern that bandits are causing trouble. The bullets have been sent to the County Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Suzhou Public Security Bureau Chief Accused of Four Counts 133

Shen Weiyang, the chief of the Public Security Bureau of Wu County, has been in office for two months and has a good reputation. He has strictly cracked down on smoking and gambling, greatly curbing the gambling atmosphere in Suzhou, which has made some people dissatisfied. Recently, Li Jinsheng and others, using their real names, filed a petition with the Department of Civil Affairs, accusing Shen of employing private individuals, engaging in improper conduct, neglecting the prohibition of smoking, and illegally requisitioning war supplies. They requested a thorough investigation. The Department of Civil Affairs is currently conducting a secret investigation, so Chief Shen has been passive in his attitude recently.

Vegetable Market Dispute Breaks Deadlock 134

The dispute over the Xiaolikou vegetable market has caused shops to strike and oppose it. Currently, all vegetable vendors are unwilling to move into the market, and there is no possibility of breaking the deadlock. In order to calm the situation, the county government has transferred the collection of donations for the project to the Second Section of the County Government, effective immediately. The construction matters will still be handled by the Technical Office, and personnel will be sent to earnestly persuade the vendors to open the market as soon as possible.

Wuxi Blackmailer Caught in Trap 135

It was decided that the master clock would be located inside the County Government, and six subsidiary clocks would be set up at the following locations: (1) Tonghui Road intersection, Class A four-sided clock post; (2) Hanchang Road middle, Class B two-sided clock post; (3) North end of Guangfu Bridge, Class A three-sided clock post; (4) Park Sheng Lane intersection, Class A four-sided clock post; (5) Chong'an Temple Mountain Gate, Class B two-sided clock post; (6) Xichengmen intersection, Class B four-sided clock post. It was decided to complete the installation within one month in order to standardize the time and cultivate the habit of punctuality among the people.

Under the Tyrannical Power of the Chongming Authorities, the Mainstay of Chongming Commentary is Arrested 140

Since the abolition of the publicly and secretly operated drug investigation bureau in this county, powerful figures from all walks of life have secretly been organizing drug manufacturing facilities. For a time, society was in an uproar, and the newspapers all had detailed reports. Among them, the Chongming Commentary Weekly was particularly able to expose all the corrupt political achievements and dark secrets from the perspective of the people, and dare to condemn them in words and writing without the slightest hesitation. Its commentary on the manufacture of drugs was even more forthright and uncompromising. Therefore, the publication was popular for a time and enjoyed great trust from people in society. However, on the evening of the 5th of the month, the captain of the 17th Squadron of the Chongming Waterborne Public Security Bureau suddenly led 40 or 50 men to arrest Lu Ping, the mainstay of the newspaper, and send him to the County Public Security Bureau. At that time, public opinion was in turmoil, and no one knew why he was arrested. Later, a reporter went to the Public Security Bureau to inquire. Director Li told the reporter that Lu was arrested and escorted by the Waterborne Public Security Team. According to the official document that the captain submitted afterwards, the reason for the arrest was defamation. In the third issue of the newspaper, in an open letter of sincere advice to the New Chong Daily, there were the following words: "New Chong Daily editors and reporters, if you go out and walk around the streets, you can always hear news about the Xisha Red Pill manufacturing factory, and what is even more surprising and you must be able to hear is that the owners of the Red Pill manufacturing factory are County Magistrate Gong, Captain, and several others. New Chong Daily editors and reporters, who boast of recording everything they hear, why don't you publish it? Could it be that you haven't heard it? No, you definitely haven't heard it, because the rumors are unreliable and they would never do such despicable and lowly things, so you don't publish it. That's right, this publication also believes that this kind of thing is absolutely not true, so even though there have been submissions commenting on this kind of thing, they have not been published. Colleagues can know that 'recording everything they hear' contains a very important condition, that is, what is heard must have at least a ×% certainty before it has any value for publication." It is also heard that the County Public Security Bureau will transfer the case to the County Judiciary for interrogation this afternoon (6th). However, after the occurrence of this case, people in society all believe that the Waterborne Public Security Team's arbitrary arrest of people is illegal. Moreover, with regard to the above-mentioned content published in the newspaper, whether it constitutes defamation is something that anyone who knows a little about writing can understand. Now, at a time when the country is protecting news reporters under a clear order, they have become ashamed and angry, disregarding the law and wanting to control public opinion and block the people's voices. Therefore, the local people are incensed by this injustice and have organized a Lu case support association preparatory committee. In addition to strongly advocating to the authorities, they are also appealing to all parties to preserve justice.

Radio Inventor Marconi Arrives in Shanghai This Afternoon; Mayor Wu and Others Will Welcome Him at the Station; Academic Groups Held a Preparatory Meeting Yesterday; A Grand Welcome Meeting Will Be Held Tomorrow 142

Radio inventor Guglielmo Marconi and his wife, after touring the world and arriving in China, took the 11:00 PM Beijing-Shanghai express train last night with the Italian ambassador to China, Pellegrino Ghigi, and will arrive in Shanghai. They are scheduled to arrive in Suzhou around 4:00 or 5:00 AM this morning to tour the city, and around 12:00 PM they will take the Beijing-Shanghai commuter train to Shanghai, arriving at the North Station around 2:30 PM this afternoon. Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng, representatives from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs office in Shanghai, and local radio education institutions are planning to go to the North Station to welcome him. Various academic groups in the city believe that Mr. Marconi's invention of radio has made a great contribution to the world, and a preparatory committee has been organized to give him a grand welcome. It has been decided to hold the meeting at 4:00 PM tomorrow (8th) at Jiaotong University. Details are as follows:

Preparatory Meeting Held Yesterday 143

Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, the committee held its third preparatory meeting at the China Science Society. Representatives from the China Science Society, the Academia Sinica, the Joint Association of Universities, the Shanghai Radio Broadcasting Station, the Engineering Society, the Chinese Arts and Crafts Society, Jiaotong University, the China Radio Engineering School, the City Education Association, the Joint Association of Secondary School Teachers and Staff, the Electric Power Public Welfare Association of the Ministry of Transportation, the International Problems Research Society, and the China Scientific Movement Society, totaling 14 groups, including Yang Xiaoshu, Yang Zhaoxiao, Li Zhaohuan, Fang Ziwei, Su Zuguo, Liu Baimin, Huang Zaoxiong, Xu Xingchu, Zhu Youhuan, Chen Jinming, Cao Zhongyuan, and others, more than 20 people, attended. After the meeting, Mr. Marconi will be invited to give a public academic lecture. In addition to the founding academic groups being able to send five representatives to participate, Mayor Wu, former President Song, Director Bo of the Education Bureau, and Director Rong of the Telegraph Bureau, as well as various consuls, foreign guests and their spouses, and Chinese and Western newspapers, have been invited to attend on time to participate in the grand event.

Election of General Assembly Officers 145

Banquet Schedule 146

The International Telecommunications Bureau will host a banquet on the evening of the 10th. Song Ziwen will welcome him at noon on the 10th. On the 11th, all employees of the Marconi Wireless Telegraph Company will host a banquet. As for Mayor Wu's personal banquet, it is said to be scheduled for the afternoon of the 9th.

Brief Biography of Mr. Marconi 147

Guglielmo Marconi, an Italian electrical engineer, is famous in the world for inventing wireless telegraphy. He was born in Bologna on April 25, 1874. In his youth, he studied under Professor Righi, a student of Leggiero. He then entered the University of Bologna, where he was influenced by Professor Righi, who was enthusiastic about researching the electric waves discovered by Hertz. Therefore, Marconi had the idea of using electric waves to transmit messages. As a result of his research, he improved various receivers. In 1895, he went to Griffon to conduct experiments on wireless telegraphy, which were very successful. The chief engineer of the British Telegraph, Preece, also praised Marconi's new method after testing it. Soon after, the Italian Navy also tested Marconi's wireless telegraphy. In 1897, the Marconi Wireless Telegraph Company was established. In 1899, England and France were able to communicate across the English Channel. Marconi's telegraph was widely used by the navies of both England and Italy. In 1903, Marconi transmitted American news to the London Times. In the same year, the "Lucania" ship was able to get world news at all times in the Atlantic Ocean, without interruption throughout the entire journey. By 1904, Cunard Company ships were publishing European and American news dailies while crossing the sea. Its application in the business world began in 1907. Marconi is not only a businessman, but the development of his business is the result of his lifelong research. He has never relaxed his spirit of progress because of his great success. In 1906, he invented a direct communication method and set up a new method of sending continuous waves. In 1910, Mr. and Mrs. Marconi (photographed by Gong Shuxian)

invented a new type of piston receiver and electro-hydraulic detector. He also devised a way to make the transmitting and receiving machines mutually transmit and receive at extremely high speeds, and the effect was as if they were simultaneously receiving and transmitting. Therefore, two messages could be sent back and forth at the same time, which is similar to the principle of multi-channel wired telegraphy. Marconi Company's telecommunications reach everywhere. Its station in Argentina can receive signals from Ireland and Nova Scotia, and its distance is no less than five or six thousand miles. Extending it to other stations in South America, the total length can reach seven thousand miles. Italy joined the war in 1915, and Marconi became the director of the Italian government's wireless telegraph administration. He was awarded the Grand Cross by the King of Italy and honors from England, France, and other countries. In 1904, he received honorary degrees from Oxford and Glasgow Universities. In 1909, he and Braun shared the Nobel Prize in Physics. Marconi's contribution to the world and the world's respect for inventors can be seen from this.
