Eight Province and City Grain Conference Held Preliminary Meeting Yesterday; Agreement Reached on Organizing Production and Sales Agencies; Formal Meeting Scheduled for 9:00 AM This Morning 151

The Eight Province and City Grain Conference held a preliminary meeting at Cuixiu Hall on Fuyou Road yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM. Representatives from all provinces and cities except Fujian and Guangdong attended the meeting. During the meeting, they exchanged opinions with each other and adjourned at around 5:00 PM. The Shanghai representatives hosted a banquet for the representatives of various provinces and cities at Xinghualou. A formal meeting will be held at 9:00 AM this morning. Details are as follows:

Representatives Arriving in Shanghai 152

The representatives who arrived in Shanghai successively the day before yesterday included: Ji Hua, representative of the Hebei Provincial Government; Wu Tixian, representative of the Jiangsu Provincial Chamber of Commerce; Wang Cheng Rong, representative of the Zhejiang Provincial Government; Zhu Huiqing, representative of the Provincial Joint Chamber of Commerce; Wu Jiantao, representative of the Jiangxi Provincial Government; Jiang Hanluo, representative of the Hubei Provincial Government; Huang Yunqing and Yao Weizhang of the Hankou Grain Industry Association; Yuan Fen, representative of the Anhui Provincial Government. There are also representatives from Hunan Province, who are still en route. Representatives from Fujian and Guangdong will not be able to attend.

Preliminary Meeting 153

Yesterday afternoon, with more than half of the attending representatives, a preliminary meeting was convened first. In addition to the above-mentioned representatives, the attendees also included Wu Huanru and Zhou Minggang, representatives of the Municipal Government; Gu Xinyi, Zhu Zixiang, Jiang Zisheng, Yan Xiaoquan, Cai Yukun, Chen Ziyi, Zhu Yunzhang, and Jiang Hongbin, representatives of the Bean and Rice Industry Association; and Feng Yongsheng, Chen Shide, and Fu Changyu, representatives of the Grain Industry Association, more than 20 people.

Mr. Gu's Report 154

After the formalities, temporary Chairman Gu Xinyi gave a report, stating that the convening of this conference was based on the grain conference convened at Chiang Kai-shek's headquarters in Nanchang. We are aware that the bankruptcy of Chinese rural areas is largely due to the uneven regulation of grain. Rice-producing areas are unable to export their surplus rice, while rice-deficient areas have no way to seek supplies, resulting in price differences, which have a very negative impact on the people's food supply. Therefore, foreign rice takes the opportunity to invade, resulting in a huge outflow of cash every year. It is proposed to levy a 90% tax on foreign rice in order to make up for this. Therefore, once the foreign rice tax is implemented, the demand for domestic rice in rice-deficient areas can be increased. Then the adjustment of production and sales also seems to be imminent. Now, it is proposed to combine the official and commercial power of eight provinces and cities to jointly organize a grain production and sales agency. However, the organization of this agency requires funding. Chiang Kai-shek has approved a government loan of one million yuan, and each province and city will raise another one million yuan. The remaining amount will be handled by the silver and money industry through mortgage or loan, with the lowest possible interest rate. In terms of transportation, the lowest possible water power will be used, sufficient to cover its coal and water costs without incurring losses. At the closing of the Nanchang conference, the representatives unanimously agreed to further discuss concrete measures. Now, all the plans have been drafted and submitted to Chiang Kai-shek for approval, who believes they can be implemented. Therefore, this city has telegraphed to invite representatives from various provinces and cities to Shanghai to discuss the matter in detail. Although not all attendees can be present, we already have a majority, so we will first hold a preparatory meeting to allow the representatives of the provinces and cities to express their high opinions first, so that all the issues can be resolved smoothly at tomorrow's formal meeting.

Exchange of Opinions 155

Following the chairman's report, representatives from various provinces and cities provided detailed reports on their respective provinces' engagement situations. They engaged in extensive discussions regarding future strategies, generally reaching a consensus. They agreed that grain production and marketing organizations were essential, deeming them best operated through joint public-private ventures, as opposed to solely by the government or merchants. They also agreed to exert full effort to facilitate the establishment of such organizations. The possibility of remedial measures for the provinces of Fujian and Guangdong, should they not participate in the organizations, was also discussed. Therefore, all issues brought up for discussion during today's formal meeting are expected to proceed smoothly.

Shanghai's Banquet 156

After the meeting adjourned, the representatives hurried back to their residences. In the interest of fostering camaraderie, the Shanghai representatives Wu Huanru, Gu Xinyi, and Zhou Minggang hosted a banquet for the representatives at Xinghualou Restaurant at 7 PM last night. All representatives attended the banquet, during which they exchanged views on the capital needed to establish future production and marketing organizations. The gathering concluded amicably around 8 PM.

The Shanghai Architectural Association, due to the Ministry of Finance's Tax Bureau implementing an increased consolidated tax on cement from the 5th of this month, raising the tax from the original 60 cents per barrel to 1.20 yuan per barrel, causing prices to soar, various member construction factories, unable to bear this significant loss, have requested discussions on coping methods. In order to improve police affairs in Guangxi Province, the Guangxi Provincial Government specially sent Jiang Fei, director of the police officer training school, and his entourage Ma Kangpin to Shanghai to investigate police affairs. Mr. Jiang arrived in Shanghai a few days ago and visited Mayor Wu to state his intentions. The municipal government instructed the Public Security Bureau to provide proper accommodation. It is reported that after Mr. Jiang completes his investigation in Shanghai, he will go to Peiping, Tianjin, and other places to continue his investigation.

Announcement of Land Value Assessment in Two Districts: Tax Collection to Begin in Two Locations from the 21st; Assessment Very Low, Annual Revenue Less Than One Million Yuan 168

The collection of land value tax in this city has been decided to be implemented from the 21st of this month. The collection area includes maps 1 to 7 in the Hunan District and maps 1 and 2 in the Zhabei District. The land value, after being assessed by the Land Valuation Committee, with a maximum and minimum value for each map, has been submitted to the municipal government for approval by the Land and Finance Bureaus, and will be officially announced today. The assessed land value and methods are recorded separately below.

Assessed Land Value 169

The land value of each map in the Hunan and Zhabei districts, after being assessed by the Valuation Committee, has been approved and announced by the municipal government as follows: (Hunan District) Map 1: highest land value 31,500 yuan, lowest land value 4,100 yuan; Map 2: highest land value 15,800 yuan, lowest land value 3,900 yuan; Map 3: highest land value 36,000 yuan, lowest land value 3,900 yuan; Map 4: highest land value 13,500 yuan, lowest land value 2,300 yuan; Map 5: highest land value 18,000 yuan, lowest land value 1,200 yuan; Map 6: highest land value 7,200 yuan, lowest land value 700 yuan; Map 7: highest land value 2,700 yuan, lowest land value 600 yuan; (Zhabei District) Map 1: highest land value 7,200 yuan, lowest land value 700 yuan; Map 2: highest land value 13,500 yuan, lowest land value 900 yuan.

Collection Methods 170

After the tax collection begins, all land in each area that has been assessed should pay the second installment of the year's actual levy of five-sixths of the land value tax. The deadline for payment is two months from the date of collection, ending on February 20, 1934. Those whose land is in the Hunan District should pay at the Southern Inspection Office of the Finance Bureau in Maojia Lane, Nanshi; those in the Zhabei District should pay at the Northern Inspection Office on Datong Road, Zhabei. Those who fail to pay within the deadline will be summoned for overdue payment.

Below Budget 171

According to Liang Sicheng, director of the Zhabei Inspection Office, the land value tax in the city, according to the initial budget, can collect one million yuan per year. However, according to the current assessed land value budget, due to the lower assessment and the reduction of the transfer tax by three-quarters, the actual collection in the future may be less than half of the initial budget. It is also said that the numbers and deadlines reported in the previous report on the slaughter tax are inconsistent and will be announced again.

Cigarette Manufacturers Hold Representative Meeting Yesterday, Resolving to Purchase and Affix New Stamps Immediately, Requesting Government to Allot Subsidy 172

Cigarette manufacturers in this city, due to the Ministry of Finance's Tax Bureau implementing newly set consolidated taxes from the 5th of this month, requested a postponement, which was not approved. The industry association held a representative meeting yesterday, deciding to accept the new tax with a heavy heart and pay taxes according to regulations, but requesting the government to allot a portion of the new tax revenue to relieve cigarette factories and subsidize their development. The details are recorded below.

New Tax Measures 173

The Ministry of Finance's Tax Bureau issued a notice to all cigarette factories stating, "To: Regarding the revision of the consolidated tax rate for domestically produced cigarettes, the order to implement it from December 5th has been received. This bureau has already sent the newly set tax amount limit price in a letter on the 2nd of this month for compliance. This tax increase, for cigarette packages that have affixed old tax stamps before December 5th, has been reported to the supervisor for factory release in accordance with regulations. For cigarette packages sold in this city, regardless of whether the cigarettes are sold after the implementation of the new tax form, the registered selling price should still be taxed according to the original grade or be reduced if the application is approved. In order to ensure that the value of the old stamp is more or less than the tax amount due for the new second grade, all are allowed to be sold uniformly. In the event of slow sales and change of transportation, the local consolidated tax bureau should be reported to for the issuance of a change of transportation certificate, so that the change of transportation can be carried out. However, in the event of re-packaging, stamp removal, or sales in non-consolidated tax areas, when requesting a tax refund, except for those whose original old tax stamp value is lower than the new second-grade tax amount due, the tax refund will still be based on the original stamp price. Those whose original old tax stamp value is higher than the new second-grade tax amount due should only be allowed to refund the new tax amount due for the cigarette to prevent fraud. In addition to the distribution, the revised cigarette consolidated tax rate table is enclosed for reference. Please refer to the tax rate table, with 50,000 cigarettes as the standard: Grade 1: selling price above 300 yuan, tax 160 yuan; Grade 2: selling price below 300 yuan, tax 80 yuan. Note: The maximum selling price of Grade 2 cigarettes, non-cigarette factory location, is allowed to be relaxed by 20 yuan, not exceeding 320 yuan. The maximum selling price of Grade 1 cigarettes is not limited."

Not a Work Stoppage 174

Since the news of the tax increase spread, it was suddenly reported that 42 cigarette factories had jointly signed a contract on the 4th and announced a work stoppage on the 5th to protest. According to a reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency, after investigating various factories yesterday, it was learned that there are a total of 53 Chinese cigarette factories in this city. Large-scale factories such as Nanyang and Huacheng are working as usual and have not stopped working. However, factories such as Zhongnan, Sanxing, Xinmin, Jiangzhe, Kunlun, Jiangnan, Changming, Minzhong, Ruilun, Delong, Huadong, Zhonghe, Huabei, Huapin, etc., because before the new tax was implemented on the 5th, all cigarette paper shops and other vendors had purchased in bulk to speculate, resulting in a sudden excess of demand over supply. The factories worked day and night to rush production, but the inventory was still sold out. After the 5th, the cigarette paper shops had sufficient stock and temporarily stopped purchasing, while the factories changed to day and night shifts, and the workers also felt tired, so they temporarily stopped working or opened a part, waiting for the market to turn around before resuming the original state. If it is said to be a protest against the tax increase, it is inevitable to misunderstand. Also, foreign companies such as British American Tobacco Company, Factory 1, 2, 3, etc., are also working as usual.

No Purchase of New Stamps 175

According to the industry, the various cigarette merchants' principles on the government's tax increase, due to the poor market conditions, have requested a temporary postponement. Whether manufacturers start or stop work has nothing to do with business. The most important thing is the inspection of goods when they leave the factory. Every time goods leave the factory, they are checked and released by the resident staff sent by the Consolidated Tax Bureau to each factory. Due to the accumulation of inventory from the double work on the 5th and 6th, all inventory had left the factory before the 5th of this month and was stored in warehouses for wholesale. Various sales agents are still operating as usual. Because various manufacturers still have new goods in stock that have not been released, no new stamps were purchased yesterday. The inspection office of the Tax Bureau in Nine Mu Land, Nanshi, was extremely crowded before the 5th, and the staff was very busy. Cigarettes were piled up on the road, and traffic was almost blocked. It has been cold and desolate since the day before yesterday.

Denying Loans 176

According to Mr. Lang of the Cigarette Factory Industry Association, the various cigarette merchants, before the new tax was implemented, requested the Ministry of Finance that, for the government's economic problems, the merchants could, as much as possible, pre-approve the purchase of stamps, and did not set how much each company would lend to the government. Now, reports say that Nanyang has approved 500,000 yuan, British American Tobacco has approved 2 million yuan, and Huacheng has approved 300,000 yuan as government loans. The Industry Association absolutely denies this. As for Yu Qiaqing and Du Yuesheng taking on the role of mediation, because the industry has not yet requested it, no mediation has been carried out.

Emergency Meeting 177

The Chinese Cigarette Manufacturers Association, due to the increase in tax rates, repeatedly requested a postponement of implementation, which was not approved. Therefore, at 2:30 PM yesterday afternoon, an emergency representative meeting was convened at the meeting place on Meibaige Road. Those who attended included Wu Tingsheng, Wu Gensheng, Shen Weiting, Yu Jiqin, Wang Qiuquan, Lu Wensun, Wang Xingtang, Wu Shentai, Bao Guangsheng, Jiang Lanting, Zhang Shankun, and Datong Wang Zijin, Asia Peng Zijin, Huaqing Sun, Fuyun Yongli Shi Chao Xiang, Da Zhonghua Chen Dehong, Cuiquan Wang Weilin, Changming Wang Yunfu, Huamei Yu Zhong'e, Shanghai Han Xushan, Minzhong Wu Xiaogan, Xinmin Lin Zicai, Lihua Xu Quanfu, Jiuyi Zheng Songru, Jinshan Yin Shunfei, Huada Hong Wei Guan, Kunlun Yu Lunxian, Da Dongnan Qiu Genglin, Zhang Xinliang, Huadong Li Xuelai, Huacheng Shen Xingde, Kefu Zhang Yunqing, Huaxin Wang Zhongying, Jiangzhe Liu Jiyun, Dexing Tao Wenkui, Fuxing Ding Boquan, Huachang Zhu Wenzhun, Nanyang Wu Tingsheng, Daizhongnan Shen Yankang, Delong Chen Xihong, etc., more than 50 people, chaired by Wu Tingsheng.

Resolutions 178

After the meeting opened, Chairman Wu Tingsheng first reported on the tax increase, the previous petitions to the Ministry of Finance, and the negotiations on the return of moldy cigarettes, restrictions on factory locations, and investigations of smuggled cigarettes. Next, Yu Jiqin spoke, saying that giving a 10% discount on the new tax first and then purchasing it in full is harmful to small factories, and it is better to directly implement the new tax. Then, Ding Boquan and others reported on the current situation. After discussion, a unanimous vote was passed: (1) Purchase new stamps immediately and affix them according to regulations; (2) Request the government to sympathize with the difficulties of businesses and allocate funds after the implementation of the new tax to be used for improving the business development or improvement of cigarette factories.

Reporting to the Bureau 179

After the resolution was passed, representatives were immediately selected: Wu Tingsheng, chairman of the Chinese Cigarette Manufacturers Association, and members Bao Gengsheng and Shen Weiting, three people, personally went to the Ministry of Finance's Tax Bureau to request to see Director Xie Qi, but Xie had gone to Hangzhou and did not meet them. It was also 5 o'clock, which was past the regulations for office hours. The three representatives reported this intention to the tax bureau staff, and the tax bureau staff promised to submit this intention to the director for review and decision, and generally felt that there would be no problem.

Retail Price Increase 180

Since the newly set tax amount for cigarettes was implemented on the 5th of this month, various cigarette factories have increased the selling prices of various cigarettes accordingly. As a result, the price of cigarettes in various cigarette paper shops has increased by about 2 copper coins for every 10-piece pack above 200 wen, and about 1 coin for those below 200 wen. A 50-piece pack has increased by 1 to 2 cents per tin. However, there are also those that have not increased in price, because the cigarettes sold in various cigarette paper shops are all inventory purchased before the 5th of this month.

New Tax Revenue 181

According to Wang, director of the cigarette section of the Consolidated Tax Bureau, and Zong, director of the accounting section, the average monthly special tax on cigarettes is about 5 million yuan, and the annual revenue is about 65 million yuan. After the Ministry of Finance newly revised the tax rate this time, it will increase by about one-third. If the situation of previous years is followed, it can increase revenue by more than 10 million yuan. As for how manufacturers express themselves, the Ministry of Finance will preside over the handling of it. This bureau is ordered to handle it, and unless the Ministry of Finance has other orders, it will definitely start collecting taxes according to the new tax rate.

Japanese Goods Arrive in Crowds: Economic Aggression Against China, Seizing Our Foreign Trade 182

In the most recent ten days, imports of Japanese goods have been extremely crowded. From the 25th of last month to yesterday, there have been six or seven Japanese ships arriving in Shanghai, loaded with Japanese goods, mainly cement, Dongtang, hardware and electrical materials, match stems, stone powder, and fabrics. There are also many seafood products. They are all transported from Rokko Maru, Mikasa, Aso Maru, etc. Each time, the number ranges from 16,000 to 17,000 pieces to 28,000 to 29,000 pieces. Seventy percent of them are unloaded in Shanghai warehouses, and two to three tenths are transferred to the Yangtze River, Changsha, and Sichuan. In total, the import of Japanese goods in this decade is more than 100,000 pieces. More than 30,000 pieces will arrive in Shanghai tomorrow and the day after tomorrow. There are also a large number of machine materials arriving. As for Japanese goods being transported to Europe and seizing our country's exports, such as soybeans, camphor, paper umbrellas, and Huzhou silk, these goods have recently been transported to Italy, causing our country's exports to Italy to plummet, all of which have been seized by Japanese goods. A large number of bicycles are also transported to Europe, selling for only 20 to 30 yuan per vehicle, so a large number are exported.

Fresh Meat Aircraft Purchase Funds Secured 183

Two-thirds of the funds for slaughter improvement are allocated by the Municipal Finance Bureau to the Shanghai Fresh Meat Industry Association to request that two-thirds of the funds for slaughter improvement be allocated to donate to aviation and purchase the Shanghai Fresh Meat Aircraft. A special report was submitted to the municipal government for instructions. The municipal government instructed the bureau a few days ago to approve the temporary termination of the Slaughter Improvement Fund Management Committee. All slaughter funds, except for two-thirds of the funds allocated for aviation donation, the remaining one-third will be used for public welfare purposes of the industry. The methods are as follows: (1) After the full amount of the aviation donation is allocated, all funds should still be used for the public welfare of the meat industry, and the competent authority will manage them separately, and the municipal government will supervise them; (2) The amount of the aviation donation, as requested, will be negotiated by the meat industry association and the aviation association.

Announcement of Regulations for Collecting House Tax: Land Value Tax Has Been Implemented; Should Not Be Borne by Property Owners 184

The regulations for collecting land value tax in this city have long been announced and implemented by the municipal government. Previously, citizens Yao Wen and others, due to the inability to bear the burden after the war, jointly petitioned the Executive Yuan to approve the Shanghai Municipal Government to temporarily postpone implementation. If it is unavoidable and must be held, then citizen representatives should be added to the valuation committee, and the house tax should no longer be borne by the landlords. It was subsequently approved that the request to postpone the land value tax should not be discussed. However, regarding the candidates for the land valuation committee and the fact that the house tax should not still be borne by the landlords and tenants, the municipal government has been ordered to consider and handle it. The municipal government has now added citizen representatives to the valuation committee. As for how to handle the house tax, it has not yet been announced, so Yao and others have jointly petitioned the municipal government to announce the method as soon as possible to show fairness. The original report is recorded below, reporting that the land value tax has been implemented, and the house tax should no longer be borne by the landlords. It should be announced as soon as possible to comfort the public. In August of this year, the temporary land value tax regulations and implementation rules were promulgated by the government, and the date for implementation was set. The landlords and others, because they had just experienced the war, requested a strict implementation, and if it was unavoidable and had to be held, then the house tax item should no longer be borne by the landlords, so as to conform to the principle of equal taxation. It was reported to the Executive Yuan for approval, and the city's temporary land value tax regulations, which had been approved by the Yuan, and the request to postpone the handling should not be considered. As for the city's house tax, which should not still be borne by the landlords and tenants, the municipal government has been ordered to consider and handle it. This is in line with the decision of the municipal government meeting in the 18th year of the Republic of China that after the land tax law is promulgated in the future, the landlords will bear the land tax, and the tenants will bear the house tax. However, the land value tax, which was previously promulgated by the government, was set to be implemented on August 1 of this year, so it seems that the house tax borne by the landlords in the past should be announced to be stopped at the same time. Since the approval, more than a month has passed, and it has not been shown that not only has the autumn house tax been completely collected, but the winter tax has also been started. The landlords are very confused, so they jointly submit a report to the government for review and approval, and announce it clearly as soon as possible. The house tax from August of this year will no longer be borne by the landlords, and those that have already been collected will be allowed to be deducted from the land value tax to be paid, so as to fulfill the promises and comfort the public. We are extremely apprehensive and await orders. Protecting the report to the Shanghai Municipal Government, the reporters Yao Wenyan, etc.

City Chamber of Commerce and Others Telegraph Request to Protect Bank Mortgage Rights: Yufeng Yarn Factory Workers Forcibly Take Out Pledged Yarn; Failure to Stop This Would Amount to Severing the Lifeline of Industry 185

Since the Henan Yufeng Yarn Factory suspended operations due to losses, the workers' demands for resumption of work have led to prolonged and unresolved disputes. In the name of maintaining livelihoods, the workers forcibly took out yarn pledged to various Shanghai banks from the factory, intending to sell it off to distribute living expenses. The City Chamber of Commerce believes that this behavior by the workers of Henan Province infringes upon the mortgage rights of third parties. It has telegraphed the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Industry, and the Chairman of Henan Province, requesting strict correction to protect mortgage rights. The original telegram is recorded below: To the Nanjing Executive Yuan, Ministry of Finance, Ministry of Industry, Chairman Liu of the Henan Provincial Government: The China, Shanghai, and Zhejiang Xingye Banks received floral yarn as collateral for loans to the Zhengzhou Yufeng Yarn Factory, stored in the factory's warehouse. Now, to provide workers with living expenses, the labor union, in conjunction with the mediation committee, forcibly took away 369 pieces of yarn pledged to the three banks and intends to sell them off. This infringes upon the mortgage rights of third parties due to the relationship between the workers and the factory, which violates the law. If creditor's rights are not protected in the future, who would dare to lend money, which would amount to severing the lifeline of industry. We implore you to correct this. Respectfully, the Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce.

The Shanghai Banking Association has also telegraphed the Central Party Headquarters, the Executive Yuan, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Finance, the Economic Commission, the Cotton Control Commission, Chairman Liu of Henan Province, and the Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce, appealing for the upholding of justice and immediate cessation of this action. The original telegram is recorded below (abbreviated): Respected Sirs: This is to inform you that our member, the China, Shanghai, and Zhejiang Xingye Banks, has stated in a letter that the Zhengzhou Yufeng Yarn Factory owes our three banks a substantial amount of loans, and the pledged floral yarn has always been stored in the Yufeng warehouse. The factory previously suspended operations due to losses, and the issue has remained unresolved for a long time. Now, according to a telegram from our Zhengzhou bank, the labor union, in conjunction with the mediation committee, suddenly forcibly took away 369 pieces of yarn stored as collateral with our bank, intending to sell them off to distribute living expenses, leaving our bank's creditor's rights unprotected. We request that you find a way to stop this from happening. Labor disputes at Yufeng should have avenues for resolution. The labor union's forcible removal of bank collateral without the local authorities stopping it will not only make it impossible for banks in the area to operate in the future, but also, at a time when the government and various provincial authorities are making efforts to promote construction and develop industry, how can we encourage banks to do their best to assist? If our government does not promptly stop this illegal action, banks will lose their security and will have no choice but to cease all industrial lending, the impact of which on the country's industrial future is unimaginable. Therefore, we appeal to you to instruct the Zhengzhou local authorities to promptly stop this and return the cotton yarn taken by the labor union, in its entirety. We earnestly hope for this and eagerly await your instructions. Respectfully, the Shanghai Banking Association.

Two Bureaus Confer on Recovering Trans-Boundary Telephone Lines: Results Obtained; Instructions Requested from the Ministry 186

Regarding the issue of telephone lines in leased territories located on roads built beyond the boundaries, although the Ministry of Communications dispatched Advisor Gu to convene several meetings with the Shanghai Telephone Bureau and the Shanghai Municipal Public Utility Bureau to discuss methods for recovering the lines, the leased territory telephone company has found it difficult to accept. After Advisor Gu of the Ministry of Communications returned to the ministry to request instructions, the ministry recently instructed the Shanghai Telephone Bureau to work with the Municipal Public Utility Bureau to hold further meetings to discuss implementation methods. It is now known that Xu Xueyu, Director of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau, and Yu Bingjian, Chief Engineer, went to the Municipal Public Utility Bureau yesterday afternoon to meet with Xu Peihuang, Director of the bureau, and Zheng Baoqing, Section Chief of the Third Section, to discuss the recovery of leased territory telephone lines in trans-boundary areas. They continued their discussions yesterday morning and have now reached a result. They will request instructions from the Ministry of Communications before negotiating with the leased territory telephone company. However, as this matter involves foreign relations, the content of their discussions has not yet been released.

One-Week Anniversary of the Shen Bao Circulating Library: Exquisite Commemorative Booklet Printed and Distributed 187

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the Shen Bao Circulating Library, with its convenient location (3rd, 4th and 5th floors of the Continental Emporium on Nanjing Road), has a very developed library system. Recently, the number of readers has exceeded 3,000, with an average of about 600 books borrowed each day, not including those who come to read in the library. As the one-week anniversary approaches, it is reported that the library will print and distribute an exquisite commemorative booklet, but will not hold any ceremonies. Instead, it will focus all its efforts on enriching the interior and enhancing work efficiency. It has already purchased more than 3,000 new books and duplicates, added 50 to 60 new magazines, and compiled a catalog of books published over the past year to facilitate searching.

Illegal Arrest of Jin Xi: City Government Decides to Lodge a Serious Protest with the Japanese Consulate; French Consul General Agrees to Notify the Japanese Consulate for Return; City Federation Issues Declaration Requesting City Government to Negotiate 188

Henan Relief Association Reduces Expenditures to Benefit Disaster Victims 194

Dyeing Industry Reopens Dispute 195

According to news from the Regulatory Committee of the Silk and Satin Dyeing Industry Association, the Shanghai Silk and Satin Dyeing Industry Association previously experienced disturbances due to the labor side's request to restore the original wine allowance agreement. After several twists and turns, the dispute was mediated by the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs. In addition to the provisions of the 1927 wine allowance price list, the prices of other new products were given according to the industry's usual practice. The prices of some new products were stamped and sealed by a notary public. At the time, both parties agreed, and the association immediately notified the industry to comply with it. Not long after, the labor side opposed this, claiming that the capital side violated the contract. The association did not change the previous pricing regulations on the principle of the 1927 wine allowance contract. The association believes that the labor side's unreasonable dispute and reopening of the dispute is regrettable. In order to eliminate this dispute, the association convened an emergency meeting yesterday and issued the following declaration to make the society understand: Since the National Revolutionary Army established Shanghai and Nanjing in 1927, workers in various industries have begun to organize labor unions, and our industry is no exception. The labor and capital sides signed an agreement to abide by it. Later, due to the impact of the Shanghai War, various industries experienced economic pain, and our industry's dyeing prices were also reduced as a result, making it difficult to maintain operations. We then sought the consent of the workers to slightly change the original wine expenses. Last month, the Silk and Satin Dyeing Industry Office requested colleagues to increase wine allowances and went on strike for a long time. The Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs mediated the result, and it was handled in accordance with the original agreement of 1927. Not long after, the labor side suddenly reopened the dispute, claiming that colleagues had violated the contract. The colleagues have been implementing the mediation agreement of the Bureau of Social Affairs and have made no changes. However, the office made a big publicity in the newspapers, saying, "Please change your face, violate the law, and destroy the contract. If you do not immediately correct it, it will stimulate an extreme and daring trend that will not be difficult to see." Our association has been implementing the mediation agreement of the Bureau of Social Affairs, so how can there be any violation of the law? Where can it be corrected? It is not difficult to understand the cause of this dispute (omitted below). This is the declaration.

Shen Linghua's Suicide: Suspicious Points Discovered After Autopsy; Allegedly Killed and Hanged on a Tree; Now Sent to the Institute of Forensic Medicine for Autopsy 203

Shen Jinhua and Shen Linghua, two brothers who were tailors from Yaojiaqiao, Yinxiang District, ran a clothing store. Their business was doing well enough to make ends meet. They had a partner, Dong Linsheng, who was introduced to a widow, Wu Qiaoshi, by Min Wangshi, the wife of Min Zixiang. Wu Qiaoshi had previously been cohabiting with Zhu Along, so there was a dispute in their love affair. On the night of the 30th of this month, Dong was staying at the Shen's house when Zhu suddenly gathered a crowd and went there, severely injuring Dong in all four limbs. Later, Dong Linsheng was sent to the hospital for treatment, and at that time, Shen Linghua suddenly disappeared. It was not until dawn that someone discovered that he had hanged himself on a tree at the end of Huasheng Road. The third section of the fifth district sent Baochang Chen Bingsong to report to the local court that day for an autopsy. Prosecutor Xiao, along with the examiner and bailiff, arrived at the scene to conduct the autopsy. They examined the body naked, front and back, and found no other injuries. The rope marks on the neck were also a symptom of a broken cheekbone, confirming that he had died by suicide. According to Baochang's report, it was also suicide. Judging from the circumstances, it was feared that the deceased had committed suicide out of fear or perhaps had unspeakable secrets. Therefore, he ordered the family to collect the body. However, in the days following the incident, newspapers reported that after Zhu Along injured Dong Linsheng, Shen Linghua was chased out and killed, and then it was faked as a hanging to cover up the murder. At the same time, the deceased's wife, Shen Chenshi, went to the court to file a complaint, stating the above. The prosecutor summoned her and told her to provide more details. If there were any knife or axe wounds, how could there be no bloodstains to hide? However, the woman claimed that there were two knife wounds on her feet, and that she was strangled to death and then hung on the tree, and requested a re-examination. The officer believed that for the sake of caution, he ordered the police to send the coffin to the Forensic Research Institute in Zhenru yesterday for an autopsy. This is indeed a strange matter.

Both Railway Administrations Pay Attention to Heating Equipment in Passenger Cars, Special Thermometers Prepared to Regulate Temperature 209

The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administrations, noting that winter is approaching and the weather is getting colder, especially at night, have ordered that the heating equipment in all passenger trains on the Beijing-Shanghai line and the Shanghai-Ping Lianyun through train and other passenger trains should be used at all times to benefit passengers. They have specially instructed all passenger inspectors and other responsible personnel to pay attention to the heating equipment while the passenger trains are running en route. If the temperature inside the passenger car exceeds the specified standard, they must immediately inform the driver to adjust the valve to ensure a suitable temperature. Station inspectors should carefully check each passenger car before the train departs to ensure passenger comfort. To regulate the temperature inside the passenger cars, they have purchased eight thermometers and ordered the station inspector at the North Shanghai Station to rotate them for use by the passenger inspectors. They have also stipulated standard temperatures and a schedule for use, and have sent circulars to all concerned to comply. In order to cope with the current traffic conditions, they have specially revised the previously stipulated schedule for using the thermometers. Seven thermometers will still be temporarily distributed by the station inspector at the North Shanghai Station for rotation, while the remaining thermometer will be kept in the safe custody of the inspector. In addition, if there is no passenger inspector on duty in the passenger car, the thermometer will be carried by the ticket inspector on duty.

Verdict in the Hong Wan Case on Nanxun Road Yesterday Morning 213

The house at No. 9 Nanxun Road was the location where Japanese national Abe Dokichi and Chinese national Li Maosong and others organized a large-scale drug manufacturing operation, producing the "Hong Wan" drug. It was previously discovered by Chief Inspector Lu Liankui, Detective Liu Shaokui, Feng Zhiming, and Song Bingzheng of the Inspector-General's Office. Ten workers, including Wu Qingsheng and Tan Afu, who were manufacturing the Hong Wan, were arrested on the spot. The Japanese national Abe Dokichi, a large quantity of "Xianma" brand and "Golden Dragon" brand Hong Wan, and the materials and equipment were taken to the Hongkou police station. Mr. Abe was sent to the Japanese authorities for punishment. Subsequently, two more suspects, Wang Chengen and Yang Changsheng, were arrested in the French Concession on Baylor Road and Avenue Joffre and sent to the First Special District Court for interrogation. Yesterday morning, Judge Liu Yugui presided over the hearing in the Third Criminal Court and sentenced Wu Qingsheng, Tan Afu, Dong Changsheng, Chen Acheng, Li Youle, Qiu Yuzhang, Wang Yulin, Wang Henian, Zhang Shengfa, and Wang Chengen to six months of imprisonment each, and Yang Changsheng to three months. The number of days of detention before the trial was determined to be two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. The Hong Wan and the raw materials and equipment used to manufacture the Hong Wan seized in the case were confiscated according to the list. Wang Jinyi was found not guilty and released immediately after the police lawyer Zhang Tianyin waived the right to appeal.

Dispute Over Chen Ruilin's Estate After His Death 220

The late lawyer Chen Ruilin, a native of Chongming, was 59 years old. He practiced law in Shanghai and resided at No. 10 Yuanchengli, Route Lafayette in the French Concession. He had married three wives in his early years, all of whom died of illness. Chen had one daughter and two sons. The eldest daughter, Chunfang, is 29 years old and unmarried. The eldest son, Shoupeng, is 18 years old, and the second son, Chouchun, is 11 years old. All were born to his former wives and are currently studying at Zhengfeng Middle School. Several years ago, Chen married Gu, a widow from the same village (53 years old), as his second wife. Gu brought a son from her previous marriage, Liu Baoxiang, who was adopted by Chen as his youngest son, renamed Shou Kang, and lived together. In October of this year, Chen pre-celebrated his 60th birthday at the Guandi Temple inside the West Gate. Relatives and friends considered it inauspicious to celebrate a birthday in a temple. On the morning of November 1st, Chen died suddenly of a stroke in his residence just after getting out of bed. He had considerable savings during his lifetime, with farmland in Chongming, Baoshan, and Qidong counties, as well as cash deposited in Jin Cheng, Shanghai, Xinhua banks and Qingkang Money Shop in Shanghai. He also owned property in Zhabei, including leased land and houses, worth nearly 40,000 gold. Therefore, all the estate documents were held by his wife, Gu Zhengfeng. After learning of his brother's death, Chen Qinglin came to Shanghai to handle the funeral arrangements. Concerned that his two young nephews and unmarried niece would be discriminated against or misappropriated by Gu, he convened a family meeting as guardian, ordering Gu to hand over Chen Ruilin's estate for safekeeping and analysis. However, Gu refused to hand over the estate, arguing that as the wife of the deceased, she had the right to inherit and manage the estate and that others should not worry about it. At this point, Chen Qinglin, in his capacity as guardian, and his two nephews hired a lawyer and published a statement in the newspaper, and sent letters to various banks, money shops, and tenants, prohibiting the deposit, receipt, and storage of various funds. On one hand, he appointed lawyer Huang Zengjie as his agent and filed a lawsuit in the Civil Court of the Second Special District Court, requesting a judgment ordering Chen Gu Zhengfeng to hand over the estate documents of Ruilin for safekeeping and analysis. Chen Gu Zhengfeng also hired lawyers Gong Chuyin and Huang Daping as her agents and filed a lawsuit in the Second Special District Court, requesting confirmation of her right to manage Chen Ruilin's estate. The court has issued summons based on the lawsuit and scheduled a hearing. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, Judge Wu Xiaoke presided over the hearing in the Seventh Civil Court. In the case of Chen Qinglin, Shoupeng, Chouchun, and others suing for an order to Chen Gu Zhengfeng to hand over the estate documents, both parties were represented by lawyers. First, the plaintiff's lawyer stated the intention of the lawsuit. The defendant's lawyer then stated that the defendant had filed a lawsuit to confirm the right to manage the estate and had received a summons for a hearing scheduled for the 8th (tomorrow). However, the two lawsuits had the same subject matter, and he requested that the court merge the two cases for trial. The judge asked the plaintiff's lawyer how much property was involved, and the lawyer replied that it was approximately 30,000 to 40,000 yuan. Because the banks had refused to provide information, the exact amount was unknown. He requested that the court send letters to the banks to inquire. He then submitted a list of assets. After the court reviewed the list, it ruled that the plaintiff's cause of action was not clear, the litigation costs had not been paid in full, and it ordered a rescheduling of the hearing after the amount of the property was determined, and ordered the plaintiff to pay the litigation costs. The plaintiff's lawyer also stated that the two plaintiffs were young and studying, and had no financial ability. If they were required to pay the litigation costs in the future, they would have to apply for legal aid. He made a verbal statement. The judge ruled that they could apply for a review when the time came and adjourned the court.

Dai Rongnai's House on Jinjiapailou Street Robbed, Pretending to Rent an Empty House, Came to Survey Twice, 1 Dollar Deposit Received, Over 300 Yuan Robbed 221

Dai Rongnai, a Ningbo businessman specializing in hardware, lived at No. 16 Ruyili, Jinjiapailou, under the jurisdiction of the Second Sub-precinct of the Nanshi Public Security Bureau. Dai himself was the landlord. Recently, two rooms in the house became vacant, and he posted a rental advertisement four days ago. Until the afternoon before yesterday, a tall man with a northern accent knocked on the door and entered. He looked around and seemed quite satisfied. He paid a deposit of one dollar. Not long after, two other men came to inspect again and left. Yesterday morning at around 10:00 AM, Dai went out on time. Dai's mother, sister-in-law, and maid were picking vegetables in the living room when the tall man led three others into the house, claiming to clean the floor. At the same time, they closed the door and took out a pistol and two knives. They drove Dai's mother and others into the back living room, tied the maid's hands behind her back, and had one of the robbers guard the door. Then, they went upstairs and arbitrarily searched and robbed the house. After about a quarter of an hour, they left with their loot. After a detailed investigation, the losses, including many clothes and jewelry, a thirty dollar silver and one suitcase, totaled over 300 yuan. They immediately reported to the Second Sub-precinct, requesting an investigation.

Report of Four Banks Preparatory Treasury on Reserve Status, 205th Issue 224

The Four Banks Preparatory Treasury is jointly established by the Yanye, Jin Cheng, Zhongnan, and Continental Banks and specializes in issuing banknotes for the Zhongnan Bank. In accordance with the treasury's issuance regulations, banknotes are issued with full reserves. The cash standard is at least 60%, and the guarantee reserve is at most 40%. A public announcement is made once a week, reviewed by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. The 205th announcement of the Shanghai Preparatory Treasury on December 2, 1933, is transcribed below: Banknotes in circulation: 28,653,637 yuan. Total reserves: 28,653,637 yuan, including cash reserves of 22,550,537 yuan and guarantee reserves of 6,103,100 yuan.

Ministry of Education Suspends Issuance of Official Documents to Fujian Province 233

(Nanjing, 6th) The Ministry of Education, upon order of the Executive Yuan, has suspended the issuance of official documents to Fujian Province, effective immediately, due to the illegal occupation of Fujian's educational institutions by the puppet government.

List of Drafting Committee Members for Normal School Curriculum Finalized 234

The Ministry of Education, in order to draft standards for the normal school curriculum, has had the responsible divisions and sections, after consultation with experts in normal school education in the country, tentatively selected dozens of people. It has prepared a list of the normal school subjects to be drafted by each member and submitted it to the Minister for approval yesterday. Around the 10th, letters will be sent to the committee members, inviting them to take on drafting tasks separately. It is said that the drafting should be completed within one month from the date of the invitation, and around the beginning of January, the drafts can be collected, scheduled, and divided into groups for meetings, hoping to establish the curriculum standards before the spring break, so that all schools can have a formal new curriculum to follow after the summer vacation. As for the normal school entrance examination, no decision has been made yet and a method will be determined after the curriculum standards are announced.

Ministry Orders the Closure of the Peiping Academy of Art and Its Reorganization as a National Art Academy; Funding Will Still Be Provided by the Academy of Art; After President Xu's Second Resignation, Presidents of Various Departments Express a New Attitude 235

Peiping Special Dispatch: After the Peiping University issue developed into a stalemate, acting President Xu Songming has expressed a firm negative stance, refusing to discuss educational administration from now on. Today, he submitted his second resignation to the Ministry of Education. Presidents of various departments also expressed a new attitude today (5th). At the same time, the Ministry of Education issued instructions to Peiping, ordering the Peiping-Tianjin Higher Education Funding Management Committee to allocate the Academy of Art's funding for the Art Academy's funding from next year, and allow the Art Academy Preparatory Office to receive the funding from the Management Committee. The details of each aspect are recorded separately as follows:

Attitudes of Various Presidents 236

The reporter interviewed the presidents of various departments of Peiping University today, and the summarized opinions are as follows: President Xu (Songming) is determined to resign, and he really has his own unavoidable difficulties. The allocation of part of the Academy of Art's funding to Peiping University is not because Peiping University wants to share the Academy of Art's funding, but because the Ministry of Education had this original idea. Initially, the Ministry of Education ordered the closure of the Academy of Art, and the intention of the closure was to help Peiping University. The Ministry of Education's Order No. 8585 stated that "The Academy of Art should be closed immediately, and the funds saved should be stored specifically and transferred to Peiping University's Agricultural, Engineering, Medical, and Business Departments for special equipment." This shows that the Ministry of Education wanted to help Peiping University, which is why this measure was taken. The closure of the Academy of Art and its reorganization as an Art Academy should require separate funding and should not be robbing Peter to pay Paul. Minister Wang (Shijie) hoped that by allocating all of the Academy of Art's funding to the Art Academy, the Art Academy could become the most perfect educational institution. The Art Academy should indeed be perfect, but Peiping University, which also belongs to the Ministry of Education, should also be improved. The Ministry of Education should take overall consideration. The Art Academy has not yet been established, and it already has 10,000 yuan in funding, which can be called extremely preferential. The original funding of the Academy of Art was 10,000 yuan, which was for a university system with a four-year graduation. Now it has been changed to an Art Academy, which is a three-year graduation. Since there are fewer classes, why is 10,000 yuan needed? (2) After the Art Academy is established, it will first recruit first-year students, and the current funding will definitely not require such a large sum of 10,000 yuan. (3) The Art Academy Preparatory Office will be established in January next year and can only enroll students in June. Is 10,000 yuan needed for the Preparatory Office's funding? It is rumored that Minister Wang will not accept the above three opinions, so the predicament of Peiping University cannot be resolved.

Ministry Orders the Funding Management Committee 237

Case: The National Peiping University Academy of Art has been ordered to close, and the Executive Yuan has approved its reorganization as the National Peiping Art Academy. The Academy's original funding and assets should be fully transferred to the Art Academy for handover. The Ministry has now appointed Yan Zhikai as the director of the Preparatory Office and established the National Peiping Art Academy Preparatory Office. The original funding of 10,000 yuan for the National Peiping University Academy of Art should be fully transferred from the University, starting from January 23, to the National Peiping Art Academy Preparatory Office for monthly receipt from the Committee. In addition to separate instructions, the order should be followed and reported. Minister of Education Wang Shijie. According to Yang Likui, a standing committee member of the Funding Management Committee, after receiving the Ministry of Education's instructions, the Committee has sent separate letters to Peiping University and the Art Academy Preparatory Office today, instructing them to comply with the Ministry's order starting from January 23.

Original Order for the Academy of Art to Be Reorganized into a College 238

Case: The University of Arts has been ordered to close, and the Executive Yuan has approved its reorganization as the National Peiping Art Academy. The College's original funding and properties should be fully transferred to the Art Academy to accept. The Ministry has now appointed Yan Zhikai as the director of the Preparatory Office and established the National Peiping Art Academy Preparatory Office. In addition to the original Arts College Property Custody Office, which should be closed by this December and transfer all remaining funds and custody of the property, about the original College of Arts funding of 10,000 yuan, should be given entirely out from the University starting from January 23, to the Art Academy Preparatory Office and received directly from the Peiping and Tianjin Higher Education Funding Management Committee. In addition to separate instructions to National Peiping Art Academy Preparatory Office, the Peiping-Tianjin Higher Education Funding Management Committee should comply with the order and report. This order, Minister of Education Wang Shijie.

Process of Reorganization of the Academy of Art into a College 239

The College of Art was originally called the Beijing Art School, which opened in April of the seventh year of the Republic of China, dividing it into secondary and higher divisions. In June of the eleventh year, it was renamed the Beijing Art College. In March of the fourteenth year, it was suspended. In the fifteenth year, it reopened and was renamed the Art College. In the seventeenth year, it was renamed the College of Art, National Peiping University, establishing six departments: Chinese Painting, Western Painting, Applied Art, Architecture, Music, and Drama. This was the most prosperous period of the College. Subsequently, opinions among the professors of each department diverged, student factions formed, and Director Xu Beihong was expelled and Secretary Jiang Yaqu was beaten. The Ministry of Education regarded the College of Art as a nest of reactionary elements. Therefore, it instructed Peiping University to close the College of Art. After the efforts of the Peiping University authorities, it was changed to a gradual closure each year. This year, the Minister of Education changed, and Wang Shijie was honored as Minister. Not long after taking office, he immediately ordered the College of Art to be closed, and the slogan of "gradual closure" was announced to be cancelled. For students whose studies were not yet complete, the Ministry of Education ordered the College of Art to issue diplomas for two or three-year specialized courses. After the mediation of Xu Songming, the acting President of Peiping University, it was finally agreed to allow some students, such as Ms. Shi Xiaoyun, to transfer to other schools, and the College of Art was ordered to be closed immediately, clearing the arrears of teachers and staff. Recently, the Ministry of Education, because the closure of the College of Art was completed, requested the Executive Yuan to reorganize the College of Art into the National Peiping Art Academy, first establishing a preparatory office and appointing Yan Zhikai as the director. This is the process of reorganizing the College of Art into a College. As for the detailed measures for the reorganization, they have not yet been announced.

Professors Express Their Attitudes 240

According to Professor Liu, there are ways to solve the funding problems of Peiping University. During Zhu Jiahua's tenure as Minister of Education, he originally intended to close the College of Art. After the closure, all of the College's funding would be allocated to Peiping University to supplement the Agricultural, Engineering, and Medical Colleges. After the efforts of Shen Yinmo, the former President of Peiping University, and Yang Zhongzi, the former Director of the College of Art, Zhu agreed to a gradual closure. After the closure, it would be reorganized into a specialized school, with part of the funding subsidizing the Agricultural, Engineering, and Medical Colleges, and the remaining part used for the Art College. This year, Wang Shijie became the Minister of Education and suddenly issued an order to rectify Peiping University during the summer vacation, stating that the College of Art had long been ordered to close and should be closed this year. In fact, the Ministry of Education had not previously ordered it to be closed, only ordered a gradual closure. Peiping University did comply with the Ministry's order to close and made arrangements for students of the Academy to transfer. This situation gradually subsided. Now that the College of Art is about to be completed, according to the Ministry of Education's orders over the years, after the College of Art is closed, it should be reorganized into a Specialized Academy, and a part of the funding should be transferred to Peiping University's Agricultural, Commercial, and Medical departments for equipment. The remaining funds should be allocated to the Art Specialized Academy. However, Minister Wang changed his policy and allocated all of the College of Art's funding to the Art Specialized Academy. Peiping University's Agricultural, Commercial, and Medical departments cannot increase their funding by a single cent. Only next year, when the Auditing Department audits the funding, will it try to help Peiping University under the name of rescue, but in fact, it is equivalent to issuing an empty check that cannot be cashed, which is useless. The funding for the College of Art was originally 10,000 yuan per month, of which 300 yuan subsidized the High School attached to Peiping University, and 150 yuan to the Peiping University President's office, totaling 450 yuan. The College of Art actually received 9,550 yuan per month. Now that all of the College of Art's funding has been allocated to the Art Specialized Academy, the funding for the Art Specialized Academy is quite sufficient. On the Peiping University side, it is even more difficult to break the deadlock. President Xu (Songming)'s resignation is detrimental to the future of Peiping University, and the four colleges of Agriculture, Engineering, Medicine, and Commerce cannot be developed at present. The College of Arts and Law may also have problems in the future. As for whether the High School will exist after the summer vacation next year, it cannot be predicted at this moment. This is because the Ministry of Education originally ordered the High School to be closed this year, but Xu Songming, the acting President of Peiping University, argued for its retention at the risk of his job. The Ministry of Education agreed to change it to next year. This issue is still pending. (5th Jin)

Jiangxi Province Holds Middle School Student Science Competition 245

(Nanchang Communication) The Jiangxi Provincial Department of Education, in order to encourage the interest of students in provincial capital middle schools in scientific research and to assess their daily learning achievements, has specifically scheduled December 16th and 17th to hold a science competition for students in provincial capital middle schools. The competition subjects are tentatively set as Mathematics, Physics, Chemistry, and Biology. A representative competition method is adopted, with each school limited to two representatives in each group. If only junior high schools are set up, two representatives can be sent; if junior and senior high schools are set up together, four representatives can be sent. However, if there are two classes in the same grade, three representatives can be selected; if there are three classes, four representatives can be selected. Each school selects representatives limited to third-year students in both senior and junior levels. Each person can register for a maximum of three subjects. The competition questions are determined by the Department of Education. All examiners, proctors, and judges are appointed by the Director of the Department. The students and schools that win the competition will be awarded separately by the Department to show encouragement. The Department of Education has now instructed the provincial capital middle schools to announce this method to inform the students.

Local News 249

Municipal Education Bureau Ordered to Forward Regulations on Military Training Hours 250

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau yesterday issued an order to the city's private senior vocational schools, stating that the Ministry of Education's Order No. 12082 stipulates that military training is a compulsory subject in high schools and above, and vocational schools should also implement it accordingly. However, vocational schools focus on vocational training, and the teaching hours of various general subjects are limited. Therefore, senior vocational schools that enroll junior high school graduates should implement two hours of military training per week in the first and second academic years, and those that enroll elementary school graduates should implement two hours of military training per week in the fourth and fifth academic years. In addition to separate orders, it is hereby urgently ordered to forward the order to all schools for compliance.

Cooperative Society Prepares to Move to New Location: Nanjing Memorial Xianzhou Cooperative Library 251

The China Cooperative Society, located at Lishui Lane, Danshui Road, Shanghai, is constructing the Memorial Xianzhou Cooperative Library in Nanjing in memory of Xue Xianzhou. Since the construction began half a year ago, the entire project has been completed. The society is scheduled to move to the library in Nanjing on the 10th of this month to conduct its business. It is currently sorting out various documents and will hold the library's opening ceremony after moving to Nanjing. It is said that this year's annual meeting is also scheduled to be held in Nanjing next spring.

Teachers and Students of Tongji Affiliated Senior Vocational School Form School Protection Association: For the Dispute over the Mortgage Loan between the Former Labor University and the Bank of Communications 254

All teachers and students of the National Tongji University Affiliated Senior Vocational School held a meeting at the school yesterday afternoon to discuss the organization of a school protection association due to the dispute over the mortgage loan between the former Labor University and the Bank of Communications. The organization is composed of nine executive committee members and three standing committee members elected by all teachers and students. The resolutions passed were as follows: (1) Telegraph the Central Political Council, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Education, the Ministry of Justice, and various local groups and the press. (2) Issue a declaration. (3) Place advertisements in major newspapers and invite the press within days to announce the process and request assistance from all sectors.

Regulations for the Zhu Mother Gu Tai Madam Memorial Scholarship 255

Zhu Qiqing, a member of the Chinese Institute of Engineers, has donated 1,000 yuan in cash to the Chinese Institute of Engineers in July 1933 to commemorate the third anniversary of the death of his late mother, Madam Gu Tai, as a fund for the Memorial Scholarship. The following four articles of the regulations are specifically formulated: (1) Name: This scholarship is named "Zhu Mother Gu Tai Madam Memorial Scholarship," abbreviated as "Zhu Mother Scholarship." (2) Fund Management: The 1,000 yuan fund of the "Zhu Mother Scholarship" shall be managed by the fund supervisor of the Chinese Institute of Engineers and deposited in the bank for interest. No one, regardless of their position, shall be allowed to use it. (3) Scholarship Use: The interest on the fund, 100 yuan per year, shall be used as the "Memorial Scholarship" and awarded to a young Chinese person who has made outstanding achievements in the study of any engineering subject and has been selected by the association's judges. (4) Application Method: The application method for the "Zhu Mother Scholarship" of the Chinese Institute of Engineers shall be announced by the association.

The Preliminary Issue of the Ministry of Education's Preparation for the Establishment of the National Institute of Physical Education 259

The preliminary issue for the Ministry of Education's preparation for the establishment of the National Institute of Physical Education is funding. Regular expenses will only be needed after the school opens, which is not an urgent need. The current urgent need is start-up funding, at least to build a gymnasium. The construction cost of the gymnasium at Central University is over 100,000, and labor costs are now higher than before. Adding staff and student dormitories to this item will cost more than 100,000. How will this cost be raised? It is said that the relevant department of the Ministry of Education and the physical education supervisor will discuss with the minister within days. After the start-up funding is available, the preparatory work will be carried out so that the school can open after the summer vacation next year. In addition, the physical education supervisor's draft of physical education materials for junior high school students is expected to be completed before the spring cold, and the materials for high school students can be finalized before the summer vacation.
